
Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) – Service in Context 065-22040405

-   Process
-   Resources

content exists.

On this page:

Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) Service in Context home page key features

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) at the service level (Service in
Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for service details (Service in
Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for viewing and/or managing aged care
services’ bank account details (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage a residential care service’s
approved places (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage a residential care service’s
approved respite care places (days) (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s
Supplement eligibility information (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s
Refurbished status (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s
Emergency situation information - (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for viewing a residential care
service’s Special payments information (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage manual adjustments for
residential care (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to search for a care recipient (Service
in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s
fees and charges information (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for home care purposes - (Service in
Context)

Registering events in the Aged Care Staff Portal (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to register residential entry events -
(Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to approve, delete, reject or update
residential entry events - (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage enteral feeding events for
residential care (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage oxygen events for residential
care (Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view additional Transition Care days
(Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view care recipients’ leave balances
(Service in Context)

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage Aged Care Funding Instruments
(ACFIs) (Service in Context)

Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) Service in Context home page key features

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Quick access options in ACSP      |
|                                   | Service in Context home page +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ACSP Service in Context home  |
|                                   | page provides quick access to the |
|                                   | most frequently used screens. The |
|                                   | ACSP Service home page only       |
|                                   | displays for the service in       |
|                                   | context, e.g. displays the        |
|                                   | selected service’s details.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key features of the ACSP Service  |
|                                   | in Context home page are the:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Main menu (Hamburger          |
|                                   |     button) - go to Step 2        |
|                                   | -   Quick find search bar - go to |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   Quick link navigation bar -   |
|                                   |     go to Step 4                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Options in main menu (Hamburger   |
|                                   | button) + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, select the icon from   |
|                                   | the top left corner of the screen |
|                                   | to access the Main menu.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The menu contains the below       |
|                                   | sections:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Staff Portal        |
|                                   | -   Service                       |
|                                   | -   Service management            |
|                                   | -   Claims                        |
|                                   | -   Payment statements            |
|                                   | -   Reports                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An extended menu (additional      |
|                                   | options) display to Service       |
|                                   | Officers:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   depending on the service      |
|                                   |     selected, or                  |
|                                   | -   when viewing care recipient   |
|                                   |     details and/or submitting     |
|                                   |     events at the care recipient  |
|                                   |     level                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Quick find search bar, go to  |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   Quick link navigation bar, go |
|                                   |     to Step 4                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Using the quick find search bar + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Quick find search bar   |
|                                   | cannot be used to search for      |
|                                   | individual care recipients.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the Quick find search bar to  |
|                                   | quickly access a specific screen. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, the Quick find search  |
|                                   | bar is located underneath the     |
|                                   | Welcome to the Aged Care Staff    |
|                                   | Portal banner.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Type the name of the screen in    |
|                                   | the search bar. A drop down list  |
|                                   | appears showing the names of all  |
|                                   | screens containing those          |
|                                   | keyword(s).                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Quick link navigation  |
|                                   | bar, go to Step 4.                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Using the quick links navigation  |
|                                   | bar + Read more ...               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Quick links navigation bar    |
|                                   | displays a list of frequently     |
|                                   | used screens. The Quick links     |
|                                   | navigation bar is located on the  |
|                                   | left hand side of the ACSP        |
|                                   | Service in Context home page.     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) at the service level (Service in Context)

Table 2

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Choose ACSP Menu option + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ACSP home page                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen – see the    |
|                                   |     Using the Aged Care Staff     |
|                                   |     Portal home page table        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Current claim                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     4                             |
|                                   | -   Finalising claims, go to Step |
|                                   |     5                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Over occupancy report - go to     |
|                                   | Step 6                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All service claims                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 7                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     8                             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the ACSP home page +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the ACSP home    |
|                                   | page using any of the following:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select Home under the Aged    |
|                                   |     Care Staff Portal section     |
|                                   | -   the ACSP home page displays   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type Home in the Quick find   |
|                                   |     search bar                    |
|                                   | -   select Go                     |
|                                   | -   the ACSP home page screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the ACSP home page, see    |
|                                   | the Using the Aged Care Staff     |
|                                   | Portal home page table.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Going to the Current claim        |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the current      |
|                                   | claim using any of the following: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim summaries panel             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the current claim      |
|                                   |     month                         |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select Current claim under    |
|                                   |     the Claims section            |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick link navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Current claim      |
|                                   |     hyperlink in the Quick links  |
|                                   |     navigation bar                |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type Current claim in the     |
|                                   |     Quick find search bar         |
|                                   | -   select Go                     |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Using the Current claim screen +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the column headings in the  |
|                                   | Current claim screen are frozen   |
|                                   | and visible for Service Officers  |
|                                   | whenever they scroll the page     |
|                                   | down to view details.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Current claim screen          |
|                                   | displays:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   service details               |
|                                   | -   claim status                  |
|                                   | -   claim month                   |
|                                   | -   approved places - displays    |
|                                   |     for flexible care and         |
|                                   |     residential care services     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Current claim screen,      |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | search the current claim          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword. Note: search results |
|                                   |     display where the keyword is  |
|                                   |     used anywhere on the record,  |
|                                   |     even if it appears in the     |
|                                   |     middle of another word        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Legend button to       |
|                                   | display code explanations         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   care recipient’s personal     |
|                                   |     details under the Care        |
|                                   |     recipient heading (care       |
|                                   |     recipient ID, family name and |
|                                   |     given name)                   |
|                                   | -   Functional capacity score     |
|                                   |     (MBI) - displays for flexible |
|                                   |     care services only            |
|                                   | -   Care setting days - displays  |
|                                   |     for flexible care services    |
|                                   |     only                          |
|                                   | -   event details under the       |
|                                   |     Events heading (entry,        |
|                                   |     departures and leave details  |
|                                   |     etc.)                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the events by Status type:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All                           |
|                                   | -   Accepted                      |
|                                   | -   Deleted                       |
|                                   | -   Held                          |
|                                   | -   Rejected                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   | -   finalise the current claim    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Finalise the current claim + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must escalate to |
|                                   | Subject Matter Experts if         |
|                                   | required for further              |
|                                   | investigation                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a claim submits successfully,  |
|                                   | a successful message displays     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An error message displays if      |
|                                   | there is an issue with the claim  |
|                                   | finalisation process              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Tolerance checks are done at the  |
|                                   | approval stage when an SME        |
|                                   | approves all Residential claims.  |
|                                   | See Step 12 in the Using the Aged |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal home page table |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A claim requires refinalisation   |
|                                   | if tolerance checks are not met   |
|                                   | and the claim is sent back by a   |
|                                   | SME                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events with a Held status   |
|                                   | will not be processed as part of  |
|                                   | the current claim’s finalisation  |
|                                   | process and may result in over    |
|                                   | occupancy issues                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Over occupancy applies to all     |
|                                   | care types except home care       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For flexible care, these entry    |
|                                   | events are due to a known timing  |
|                                   | issue with over lapping periods   |
|                                   | of care. That is, the care        |
|                                   | recipient has entered into care   |
|                                   | of the new aged care service but  |
|                                   | a departure event has not been    |
|                                   | submitted by the previous aged    |
|                                   | care service                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are resolved   |
|                                   | when Services Australia has       |
|                                   | received the departure event from |
|                                   | the previous aged care service    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the over occupancy report      |
|                                   | message and report displays, this |
|                                   | will prevent Service Officers     |
|                                   | from finalising the claim         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The over occupancy issue must be  |
|                                   | resolved before the claim can be  |
|                                   | resubmitted                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To assist in resolving the over   |
|                                   | occupancy issue, Service Officers |
|                                   | can select the Over occupancy     |
|                                   | report option to identify:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the specific care recipients  |
|                                   |     causing the over occupancy    |
|                                   | -   the number of approved places |
|                                   |     over occupied (the number of  |
|                                   |     care recipients over          |
|                                   |     occupied)                     |
|                                   | -   total occupancy               |
|                                   | -   approved occupancy            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Current claim screen,      |
|                                   | Service Officers can finalise the |
|                                   | current claim by selecting the    |
|                                   | Finalise claim button.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A warning message displays:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ‘WARNING: The claim may contain   |
|                                   | outstanding events with a status  |
|                                   | of being:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   processed, or                 |
|                                   | -   held                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These may or may not be           |
|                                   | subsequently accepted and         |
|                                   | included within this claim for    |
|                                   | payment. Do you want to finalise  |
|                                   | the claim for [month year] with   |
|                                   | these events outstanding?’        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, select Submit to finalise    |
|                                   | the claim                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 6 if the claim     |
|                                   |     finalisation process is       |
|                                   |     unsuccessful due to over      |
|                                   |     occupancy issues              |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends if the         |
|                                   |     successful receipt message    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, to cancel the claim           |
|                                   | finalisation process              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Current claim screen will |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Using the Over occupancy report + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Current claim screen,      |
|                                   | select Over occupancy report      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Over occupancy report         |
|                                   | displays:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Over occupied details             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Over occupied date - Service  |
|                                   |     Officers can select the       |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Over occupied     |
|                                   |     date and the Over occupancy   |
|                                   |     report screen will display    |
|                                   | -   Type of places                |
|                                   | -   Details                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service places over occupancy     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Places over occupied          |
|                                   | -   Total occupancy               |
|                                   | -   Approved occupancy            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Respite over occupancy            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Respite over occupied         |
|                                   | -   Respite approved occupancy    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To assist in resolving the over   |
|                                   | occupancy issue, Service Officers |
|                                   | can use the Over occupancy report |
|                                   | screen to identify:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the specific care recipients  |
|                                   |     causing the over occupancy    |
|                                   | -   the number of approved places |
|                                   |     over occupied (the number of  |
|                                   |     care recipients over          |
|                                   |     occupied)                     |
|                                   | -   total occupancy               |
|                                   | -   approved occupancy            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must contact the |
|                                   | service providers to advise which |
|                                   | care recipients or places are     |
|                                   | over occupied. The service        |
|                                   | providers must resolve the over   |
|                                   | occupancy through their current   |
|                                   | process. Once the over occupancy  |
|                                   | issue is resolved, the claim must |
|                                   | be finalised again.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     display from the Show records |
|                                   |     drop down list (bottom left   |
|                                   |     corner of the screen)         |
|                                   | -   select Back to current claim  |
|                                   |     to return to the Current      |
|                                   |     claim screen                  |
|                                   | -   download the over occupancy   |
|                                   |     report to view in an Excel    |
|                                   |     format                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Going to the All service claims   |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the All service claims screen |
|                                   | to view and/or check the status   |
|                                   | of all claims (current and        |
|                                   | historical claims) for the        |
|                                   | service in context.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the ACSP Service in Context    |
|                                   | home page, go to the All service  |
|                                   | claims screen using any of the    |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Main menu (Hamburger button)  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu          |
|                                   | -   Select All service claims     |
|                                   |     under the Claims section      |
|                                   | -   The All service claims screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the Quick find navigation bar     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type All service claims in    |
|                                   |     the Quick find search bar     |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The All service claims screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Using the All service claims      |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The All service claims screen,    |
|                                   | displays the claim history in the |
|                                   | below table format:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim month - select the up   |
|                                   |     or down arrows to display the |
|                                   |     months in ascending or        |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Date finalised - select the   |
|                                   |     up or down arrows to display  |
|                                   |     the dates in ascending or     |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Authorised person - select    |
|                                   |     the up or down arrows to      |
|                                   |     display the authorised        |
|                                   |     person’s name in alphabetical |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   | -   Channel - Services Australia  |
|                                   |     (Service Officers) or the     |
|                                   |     Portal (the aged care         |
|                                   |     service). Select the up or    |
|                                   |     down arrows to display the    |
|                                   |     Channel form in alphabetical  |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   | -   Date approved - select the up |
|                                   |     or down arrows to display the |
|                                   |     dates in ascending or         |
|                                   |     descending order              |
|                                   | -   Status - Approved, Open or    |
|                                   |     Processing. Select the up or  |
|                                   |     down arrows to display the    |
|                                   |     Status type in alphabetical   |
|                                   |     order                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | search for a specific or current  |
|                                   | claim                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   |     Note: search results display  |
|                                   |     where the keyword is used     |
|                                   |     anywhere on the record, even  |
|                                   |     if it appears in the middle   |
|                                   |     of another word               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | change the claim year             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the year from the      |
|                                   |     Claims for year drop down     |
|                                   |     list                          |
|                                   | -   the Claims for year defaults  |
|                                   |     to the current year           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records      |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for service details (Service in Context)

Table 3

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Choose ACSP menu options + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service details                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service contact details           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service approved places           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 11                       |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 12                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Financial year payments           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 13                       |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     14                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the Service details      |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Service      |
|                                   | details screen using any of the   |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   select Service details under  |
|                                   |     the Service management        |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   the Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick link navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Service details    |
|                                   |     hyperlink in the Quick links  |
|                                   |     navigation bar                |
|                                   | -   the Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   type Service details in the   |
|                                   |     Quick find search bar         |
|                                   | -   select Go                     |
|                                   | -   the Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Viewing the Service details       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must use ACMPS   |
|                                   | to view the historical service    |
|                                   | details and/or historical         |
|                                   | provider details information      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Manage aged care service  |
|                                   |     details for the process       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Service details screen        |
|                                   | displays for the service in       |
|                                   | context and is a view only        |
|                                   | screen. The Department of Health  |
|                                   | and Aged Care updates the         |
|                                   | information in the screen. This   |
|                                   | information flows from ACMPS via  |
|                                   | the NAPS gateway.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Service details screen        |
|                                   | displays the below information:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service banner - displays the     |
|                                   | Service's name, NAPS ID, RACS ID  |
|                                   | (applicable to residential        |
|                                   | services) and Service type        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service NAPS ID               |
|                                   | -   Service RACS ID               |
|                                   | -   Service BP ID                 |
|                                   | -   Service name                  |
|                                   | -   Service start date            |
|                                   | -   Service end date - displays   |
|                                   |     if applicable                 |
|                                   | -   Certified from date           |
|                                   | -   Certified to date             |
|                                   | -   Accredited from date          |
|                                   | -   Accredited to date            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Street address                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Address                       |
|                                   | -   Suburb                        |
|                                   | -   State Postcode                |
|                                   | -   Country                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact - displays the service    |
|                                   | contact details registered for    |
|                                   | the service                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Status snapshot – displays the:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   service’s status e.g.         |
|                                   |     operational, not operational, |
|                                   |     inactive or closed            |
|                                   | -   Refurbished status for        |
|                                   |     residential services only     |
|                                   | -   service’s aggregate           |
|                                   |     (combined) home care account  |
|                                   |     balance (displays for home    |
|                                   |     care services only)           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Postal address                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Address                       |
|                                   | -   Suburb                        |
|                                   | -   State Postcode                |
|                                   | -   Country                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Provider relationship             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Relationship                  |
|                                   | -   Provider name                 |
|                                   | -   Provider BP ID                |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | -   complete the Primary phone    |

|                                   |     field                         |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |

| 14                                | Using the Financial year payments |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use the      |
|                                   | Financial year payments screen to |
|                                   | generate a report displaying the  |
|                                   | number and value of aged care     |
|                                   | payments paid to the service by   |
|                                   | financial year. This report can   |
|                                   | also be downloaded in a CSV       |
|                                   | format.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Financial year payments       |
|                                   | screen will display reports going |
|                                   | as far back as follows, for the   |
|                                   | following care types:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Home care - July 2014 claim   |
|                                   |     month                         |
|                                   | -   Flexible care - March 2020    |
|                                   |     claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Residential care - July 2015  |
|                                   |     claim month                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Financial year payments       |
|                                   | screen displays the following     |
|                                   | fields:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claim month - selecting the claim |
|                                   | month’s hyperlink will take       |
|                                   | Service Officers to that relevant |
|                                   | claim month’s payment statement   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Advance payment                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Certification date i.e. the   |
|                                   |     date the advance was approved |
|                                   | -   Advance amount paid           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Final claim payment               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Certification date, i.e. the  |
|                                   |     date the claim was approved   |
|                                   | -   Payment held over i.e. any    |
|                                   |     amount the service owes to    |
|                                   |     Services Australia            |
|                                   | -   Claim amount paid             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Total amount paid                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   apply the filter criteria to  |
|                                   |     filter the reports by         |
|                                   |     financial years               |
|                                   | -   select the CSV button to      |
|                                   |     download the financial year   |
|                                   |     payments report               |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal for viewing and/or managing aged care services’ bank account details (Service in Context)

Table 4

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Choose options available in the   |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use this process table to:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | manage residential care services’ |
|                                   | bank account details in the Aged  |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP)          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view flexible care services’ and  |
|                                   | home care services’ bank account  |
|                                   | details in the ACSP               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Flexible care services’ and   |
|                                   |     home care services’ bank      |
|                                   |     account details are managed   |
|                                   |     in Aged Care Management       |
|                                   |     Payment System (ACMPS). See   |
|                                   |     the Manage bank account       |
|                                   |     details in ACMPS table for    |
|                                   |     the process                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: ACSP will display different |
|                                   | screen names depending on the     |
|                                   | care type                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following         |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Bank account summary/Bank account |
|                                   | details                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screens - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the Bank account      |
|                                   |     details screen - go to Step 3 |
|                                   | -   Using the Bank account        |
|                                   |     summary screen - go to Step 4 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View bank details                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 5                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen - go to Step |
|                                   |     6                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register bank details - go to     |
|                                   | Step 7                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Approve or reject bank details -  |
|                                   | go to Step 8                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inactivate (end date) bank        |
|                                   | details - go to Step 9            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the Bank account summary |
|                                   | screen/Bank account details       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ACSP will display different   |
|                                   |     screen names depending on the |
|                                   |     care type                     |
|                                   | -   The Bank account details      |
|                                   |     screen displays for flexible  |
|                                   |     and home care services        |
|                                   | -   The Bank account summary      |
|                                   |     screen displays for           |
|                                   |     residential care services     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Bank account |
|                                   | details/Bank account summary      |
|                                   | screen using any of the           |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Bank account details or   |

|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find search bar             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type Bank account summary in  |
|                                   |     the Quick find search bar     |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The Bank account details or   |
|                                   |     Bank account summary screen   |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick links navigation bar        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Service details    |
|                                   |     hyperlink in the Quick links  |
|                                   |     navigation bar                |
|                                   | -   The Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Service Management menu   |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   Select Bank account summary   |
|                                   | -   The Bank account details or   |
|                                   |     Bank account summary screen   |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service management tab            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Service details under  |
|                                   |     the Service Management        |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Service Management menu   |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   Select Bank account summary   |
|                                   | -   The Bank account details or   |
|                                   |     Bank account summary screen   |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   view the Bank account details |
|                                   |     screen for flexible and home  |
|                                   |     care services, go to Step 3   |
|                                   | -   use the Bank account summary  |
|                                   |     screen for residential care   |
|                                   |     services, go to Step 4        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Viewing the Bank account details  |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bank account details screen:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   is a view only screen for     |
|                                   |     flexible care and home care   |
|                                   |     services                      |
|                                   | -   displays for the service in   |
|                                   |     context                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For a residential care’s bank     |
|                                   | account details, go to Step 4     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bank account details screen   |
|                                   | displays the following table:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Verified by                   |
|                                   | -   Verified date                 |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword. Search results       |
|                                   |     display where the keyword is  |
|                                   |     used anywhere on the record,  |
|                                   |     even if it appears in the     |
|                                   |     middle of another word        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Using the Bank account summary    |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bank account summary screen:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   applies to residential care   |
|                                   |     services only                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | displays for the service in       |
|                                   | context                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The No records available          |
|                                   | information message will display: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Current bank account       |
|                                   | details table for services who    |
|                                   | have not registered their bank    |
|                                   | account details, or               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | in the Historical bank account    |
|                                   | details table if bank account     |
|                                   | details have never been           |
|                                   | inactivated (end dated)           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For a flexible care service’s or  |
|                                   | home care service’s bank account  |
|                                   | details, go to Step 2             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bank account summary screen   |
|                                   | displays the following tables:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Current bank account details      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Approved by                   |
|                                   | -   Approved date                 |
|                                   | -   Status - select the relevant  |
|                                   |     hyperlinked status to View    |
|                                   |     bank details. Go to Step 6    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Historical bank account details   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Approved/rejected by          |
|                                   | -   Approved/rejected date        |
|                                   | -   Inactive date - displays the  |
|                                   |     date when the bank account    |
|                                   |     details were inactivated (end |
|                                   |     dated)                        |
|                                   | -   Status - select the relevant  |
|                                   |     hyperlinked status to View    |
|                                   |     bank details. Go to Step 6    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Register bank details. |
|                                   |     Go to Step 7                  |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword. Search results       |
|                                   |     display where the keyword is  |
|                                   |     used anywhere on the record,  |
|                                   |     even if it appears in the     |
|                                   |     middle of another word        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
