+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Using the View bank details       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View bank details screen      |
|                                   | displays for residential care     |
|                                   | services only                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A different user to the one who   |
|                                   | either registered (created)       |
|                                   | and/or updated the bank account   |
|                                   | details can approve or reject the |
|                                   | record                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Bank account details with the:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Pending approval status can   |
|                                   |     be approved or rejected       |
|                                   | -   Approved status can be        |
|                                   |     inactivated (end dated)       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View bank details screen      |
|                                   | displays the details for an       |
|                                   | individual bank account record.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View bank details screen      |
|                                   | displays the following            |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Registered by                 |
|                                   | -   Registered date               |
|                                   | -   Approved/rejected by          |
|                                   | -   Approved/rejected date        |
|                                   | -   Inactivated by                |
|                                   | -   Inactive date                 |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Approve - go to Step 8        |
|                                   | -   Reject - go to Step 8         |
|                                   | -   Inactivate - go to Step 9     |
|                                   | -   select Go to Bank account     |
|                                   |     summary to return to the Bank |
|                                   |     account summary screen        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Register bank details + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step applies to residential  |
|                                   | care services only                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bank name field appears after |
|                                   | valid Bank State Branch (BSB)     |
|                                   | details have been provided in the |
|                                   | BSB* field                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After Service Officers have       |
|                                   | registered bank account details,  |
|                                   | they need to be approved before   |
|                                   | they can be used                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Subject Matter Experts (SME)      |
|                                   | and/or Team Leaders in the Aged   |
|                                   | Care Payments Team (Aged Care and |
|                                   | Allied Health Branch) with the    |
|                                   | following security roles have the |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | residential care services’ bank   |
|                                   | account details                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor                       |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Team Coach Manager  |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A different user to the one who   |
|                                   | registered (created) the bank     |
|                                   | account details can approve or    |
|                                   | reject the record                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | New bank account details cannot   |
|                                   | be registered if there are        |
|                                   | already bank account details      |
|                                   | pending approval                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Before registering a service’s    |
|                                   | bank account details, Service     |
|                                   | Officers must assess the          |
|                                   | completed AC015 form received via |
|                                   | email or PaNDA.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Checking the Application to |
|                                   | add or change Approved Aged Care  |
|                                   | Service’s bank details form       |
|                                   | (AC015) of Bank account details   |
|                                   | for aged care services to do      |
|                                   | this.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the AC015 form has not been    |
|                                   | assessed as complete:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Contact the aged care service |
|                                   |     and request them to resubmit  |
|                                   |     the AC015 form as a matter of |
|                                   |     urgency                       |
|                                   | -   See Checking the Application  |
|                                   |     to add or change Approved     |
|                                   |     Aged Care Service’s bank      |
|                                   |     details form (AC015), Step 2  |
|                                   |     of Bank account details for   |
|                                   |     aged care services for the    |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Once the resubmitted form has |
|                                   |     been assessed for completion, |
|                                   |     continue with this step       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Bank account summary     |
|                                   | screen, select Register bank      |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Register bank details screen  |
|                                   | displays the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   BSB*                          |
|                                   | -   Account number*               |
|                                   | -   Account name*                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Register bank details,         |
|                                   | complete the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   BSB* - key the 6 digit BSB    |
|                                   |     number and do not include the |
|                                   |     hyphen. Service Officers can  |
|                                   |     either press Enter or move    |
|                                   |     their mouse pointer to the    |
|                                   |     Account number* field to      |
|                                   |     allow for ACSP’s automatic    |
|                                   |     BSB verification process to   |
|                                   |     occur                         |
|                                   | -   Account number* - key the     |
|                                   |     bank account number and do    |
|                                   |     not include the hyphen        |
|                                   | -   Account name* - key the bank  |
|                                   |     account name                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register bank        |
|                                   | details process?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The Register? pop up          |
|                                   |     notification displays         |
|                                   | -   Select Yes in the Register?   |
|                                   |     pop up notification           |
|                                   | -   The Receipt screen displays   |
|                                   |     the SUCCESS: Bank details are |
|                                   |     registered and pending        |
|                                   |     approval information message  |
|                                   | -   Select Go to bank account     |
|                                   |     summary to return to the Bank |
|                                   |     account summary screen        |
|                                   | -   The newly registered bank     |
|                                   |     account details’ status       |
|                                   |     reflects as Pending approval  |
|                                   |     in the Current bank account   |
|                                   |     details table                 |
|                                   | -   The Service Officer must      |
|                                   |     advise a SME or a Team Leader |
|                                   |     to approve or reject bank     |
|                                   |     account details               |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here for the   |
|                                   |     Service Officers              |
|                                   | -   For SMEs and/or Team Leader   |
|                                   |     with the appropriate security |
|                                   |     roles, go to Step 8 to        |
|                                   |     approve or reject bank        |
|                                   |     account details               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   The Cancel? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification displays         |
|                                   | -   Select Yes in the Cancel? pop |
|                                   |     up notification to return to  |
|                                   |     the Bank account summary      |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Approve or reject bank details    |
|                                   | pending approval + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step applies to residential  |
|                                   | care services only                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SMEs and/or Team Leader in the    |
|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |
|                                   | with the following security roles |
|                                   | have the authority to do this     |
|                                   | step                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor                       |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Team Coach Manager  |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A different user to the one who   |
|                                   | registered (created) or updated   |
|                                   | the bank account details must     |
|                                   | approve or reject the bank        |
|                                   | account details                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The bank account details’ status  |
|                                   | remains as Pending approval if No |
|                                   | is selected in either the         |
|                                   | Approve? or Reject? pop up        |
|                                   | notification                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Bank account summary     |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the hyperlink Pending      |
|                                   | approval status in the Current    |
|                                   | bank account details table        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the View bank details screen      |
|                                   | displays the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date - this field   |
|                                   |     is blank until the bank       |
|                                   |     account details are approved  |
|                                   | -   Registered by -               |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the log   |
|                                   |     on ID of the staff who        |
|                                   |     registered the bank account   |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   Registered date -             |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the date  |
|                                   |     on which the bank account     |
|                                   |     details were registered       |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected by - this   |
|                                   |     field is blank until the bank |
|                                   |     account details are           |
|                                   |     approved/rejected             |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected date - this |
|                                   |     field is blank until the bank |
|                                   |     account details are           |
|                                   |     approved/rejected             |
|                                   | -   Inactivated by - this field   |
|                                   |     is blank until the bank       |
|                                   |     account details are           |
|                                   |     inactivated (end dated)       |
|                                   | -   Inactive date - this field is |
|                                   |     blank until the bank account  |
|                                   |     details are inactivated (end  |
|                                   |     dated)                        |
|                                   | -   Status - displays as Pending  |
|                                   |     approval                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Approve:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Approve on the View bank   |
|                                   | details screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Approve? pop up notification  |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The ‘SUCCESS: the bank        |
|                                   |     account details have been     |
|                                   |     approved’ information message |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date -              |
|                                   |     auto-populates based on the   |
|                                   |     date the bank account details |
|                                   |     were approved                 |
|                                   | -   Registered by                 |
|                                   | -   Registered date               |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected by -        |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the log   |
|                                   |     on ID of the staff who        |
|                                   |     approved the bank account     |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected date -      |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the date  |
|                                   |     on which the bank account     |
|                                   |     details were approved         |
|                                   | -   Status - displays as Approved |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to bank account summary |
|                                   | screen to display the Go to bank  |
|                                   | account summary screen            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The bank account details’ status  |
|                                   | has been updated to Approved in   |
|                                   | the Current bank account details  |
|                                   | table                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Reject:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Reject on the View bank    |
|                                   | details screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Reject? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The ‘SUCCESS: the bank        |
|                                   |     account details have been     |
|                                   |     rejected’ information message |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date - will be      |
|                                   |     blank                         |
|                                   | -   Registered by                 |
|                                   | -   Registered date               |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected by -        |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the log   |
|                                   |     on ID of the staff who        |
|                                   |     rejected the bank account     |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected date -      |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the date  |
|                                   |     on which the bank account     |
|                                   |     details were rejected         |
|                                   | -   Status - displays as Rejected |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to bank account summary |
|                                   | to display the Go to bank account |
|                                   | summary screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The bank account details’ status  |
|                                   | has been updated to Rejected in   |
|                                   | the Historical bank account       |
|                                   | details table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Inactivate (end date) bank        |
|                                   | details + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This step applies to              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   residential care services     |
|                                   |     only                          |
|                                   | -   current bank account details  |
|                                   |     with Approved status          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SMEs and/or Team Leaders in the   |
|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |
|                                   | with the following security roles |
|                                   | have the authority to do this     |
|                                   | step                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor                       |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Team Coach Manager  |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inactivate (end date) is used     |
|                                   | when there are issues with a      |
|                                   | residential care service’s        |
|                                   | current bank account details, and |
|                                   | Services Australia has not        |
|                                   | received new details from the     |
|                                   | residential care service to       |
|                                   | replace the current details       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   After the Inactivate (end     |
|                                   |     date) process is complete and |
|                                   |     Services Australia has        |
|                                   |     received new bank account     |
|                                   |     details, Service Officers     |
|                                   |     must repeat the Register bank |
|                                   |     details process for payments  |
|                                   |     to occur                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The bank account details’ status  |
|                                   | remains as Approved and displays  |
|                                   | in the Current bank account       |
|                                   | details table if No is selected   |
|                                   | in the Inactivate? pop up         |
|                                   | notification                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Bank account summary     |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the hyperlink Approved     |
|                                   | status in the Current bank        |
|                                   | account details table             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View bank details screen      |
|                                   | displays the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Registered by                 |
|                                   | -   Registered date               |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected by          |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected date        |
|                                   | -   Inactivated by - this field   |
|                                   |     will be blank                 |
|                                   | -   Inactive date - this field    |
|                                   |     will be blank                 |
|                                   | -   Status - displays as Approved |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Inactivate                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Inactivate? pop up            |
|                                   | notification displays             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Inactivate (end date) the      |
|                                   | current bank account details:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The SUCCESS: the bank account |
|                                   |     details have been inactivated |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   Bank name                     |
|                                   | -   BSB                           |
|                                   | -   Account number                |
|                                   | -   Account name                  |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Registered by                 |
|                                   | -   Registered date               |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected by          |
|                                   | -   Approved/Rejected date        |
|                                   | -   Inactivated by -              |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the log   |
|                                   |     on ID of the staff who        |
|                                   |     inactivated (end dated) the   |
|                                   |     bank account details          |
|                                   | -   Inactive date -               |
|                                   |     auto-populates with the date  |
|                                   |     on which the bank account     |
|                                   |     details were inactivated (end |
|                                   |     dated)                        |
|                                   | -   Status - remains as Approved  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to bank account summary |
|                                   | to display the Go to bank account |
|                                   | summary screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Current bank account details  |
|                                   | table will display the No records |
|                                   | available information message     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The inactivated (end dated) bank  |
|                                   | account details will display in   |
|                                   | the Historical bank account       |
|                                   | details table with the date it    |
|                                   | was inactivated in the Inactive   |
|                                   | date field                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage a residential care service’s approved places (Service in Context)

Table 5 - this table is only for Programme Officers with the following
security roles:

-   the Department of Health and Aged Care NAPS Maintainer and Manager
-   Services Australia Business Administrator
-   Services Australia IT System Administrator

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process table applies to     |
|                                   | residential care services only    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Department of Health and Aged |
|                                   | Care is responsible for updating  |
|                                   | approved places when a            |
|                                   | residential care service goes     |
|                                   | offline for a certain period due  |
|                                   | to renovations or other reasons   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   This process is also known as |
|                                   |     applying an interruption of   |
|                                   |     service                       |
|                                   | -   The Department of Health and  |
|                                   |     Aged Care will contact the    |
|                                   |     residential care service      |
|                                   |     about confirming the          |
|                                   |     application of an             |
|                                   |     interruption of service       |
|                                   | -   As part of this confirmation, |
|                                   |     the Department of Health and  |
|                                   |     Aged Care will advise the     |
|                                   |     residential care service they |
|                                   |     must continue to submit       |
|                                   |     claims each month during the  |
|                                   |     offline period (that is,      |
|                                   |     continue to submit $0 claims) |
|                                   | -   The Department of Health and  |
|                                   |     Aged Care may also require    |
|                                   |     the residential care service  |
|                                   |     to confirm the end date of    |
|                                   |     the offline period            |
|                                   | -   The Department of Health and  |
|                                   |     Aged Care is responsible for  |
|                                   |     updating approved places to   |
|                                   |     reflect all offline places as |
|                                   |     ‘online’ places               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service approved places           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     3                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View approved places              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     5                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Extra service wards summary       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 6                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     7                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register approved places          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 8                        |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     9                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update approved places            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen, go to    |
|                                   |     Step 11                       |
|                                   | -   Using the screen, go to Step  |
|                                   |     12                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Delete approved places, go to     |
|                                   | Step 13                           |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   The Approved places record    |

|                                   |     screen displays               |

|                                   |     places record will display as |
|                                   |     Deleted in the Historical     |
|                                   |     respite care places (days)    |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The View approved places      |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage a residential care service’s approved respite care places (days) (Service in Context)

Table 6: only Department of Health and Aged Care staff can undertake
this process table

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process table applies to     |
|                                   | residential care services only.   |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | the Current and future respite    |

|                                   |     or No                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Department of Health and Aged |
|                                   | Care staff member can select      |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Respite care places       |
|                                   |     (days) record has been        |

|                                   |     places (days) section         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The View approved places      |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s Supplement eligibility information (Service in Context)

Table 7

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Options available in the Aged     |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP) + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use this process table to view    |
|                                   | all the current and historical    |
|                                   | supplements a residential care    |
|                                   | service is currently receiving    |
|                                   | and/or have received in the past. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Supplement eligibility  |
|                                   | screen is a view only screen.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following         |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Supplement eligibility            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen - go to    |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the Supplement           |
|                                   | eligibility screen + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Supplement   |
|                                   | eligibility screen using any of   |
|                                   | the following:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Supplement eligibility |
|                                   |     under the Service management  |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Supplement eligibility    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find search bar             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type Supplement eligibility   |
|                                   |     in the Quick find search bar  |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The Supplement eligibility    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service management tab            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Service details under  |
|                                   |     the Service Management        |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Service Management menu   |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   Select Supplement eligibility |
|                                   | -   The Supplement eligibility    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Viewing the Supplement            |
|                                   | eligibility screen + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use the      |
|                                   | Supplement eligibility screen to  |
|                                   | view all the current and          |
|                                   | historical supplements a          |
|                                   | residential care service is       |
|                                   | currently receiving and/or have   |
|                                   | received in the past.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Supplement eligibility screen |
|                                   | displays for residential care     |
|                                   | services.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Depending on the service’s        |
|                                   | eligibility, this screen may      |
|                                   | display the following             |
|                                   | supplements:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Accommodation charge top-up   |
|                                   |     supplement                    |
|                                   | -   Charge exempt supplement      |
|                                   | -   Clean energy supplement       |
|                                   |     (previously basic daily fee   |
|                                   |     supplement)                   |
|                                   | -   Concessional/ assisted        |
|                                   |     resident supplement           |
|                                   | -   Ex-hostel supplement          |
|                                   | -   Homelessness and Indigenous   |
|                                   |     supplements                   |
|                                   | -   Veterans' supplement          |
|                                   | -   Veterans’ Supplement          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Supplements and subsidies     |
|                                   | screen displays the following:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Current supplements and subsidies |
|                                   | results table                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Eligibility                   |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Source                        |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Historical supplements and        |
|                                   | subsidies results table           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Eligibility                   |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Source                        |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select the   |
|                                   | number of records to display from |
|                                   | the Show records drop down list   |
|                                   | (bottom left corner of the        |
|                                   | screen).                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view a residential care service’s Refurbished status (Service in Context)

Table 8

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Choose menu options in the Aged   |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP) + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Department of Health    |
|                                   | and Aged Care automatically sends |
|                                   | Refurbished status information to |
|                                   | Services Australia.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use this process table to view a  |
|                                   | residential care service’s        |
|                                   | refurbished status.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following         |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refurbished status                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen - go to    |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the Refurbished status   |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Refurbished  |
|                                   | status screen using any of the    |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Refurbished status     |
|                                   |     under the Service management  |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Refurbished status screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find search bar             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type Refurbished status in    |
|                                   |     the Quick find search bar     |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The Refurbished status screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service management tab            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Service details under  |
|                                   |     the Service Management        |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Service details screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Service Management menu   |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   Select Refurbished status     |
|                                   | -   The Refurbished status screen |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Viewing the Refurbished status    |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The No refurbished status for     |
|                                   | this service information message  |
|                                   | will display when either:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Department of Health and  |
|                                   |     Aged Care deleted the         |
|                                   |     service’s Refurbished status  |
|                                   |     record, or                    |
|                                   | -   the service has no current    |
|                                   |     and/or prior records of       |
|                                   |     refurbished status            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When the Department of Health and |
|                                   | Aged Care update or delete the    |
|                                   | service’s Refurbished status      |
|                                   | record, the Refurbished status    |
|                                   | section will display the          |
|                                   | updated/deleted reason and the    |
|                                   | Refurbished status history        |
|                                   | details will display the history  |
|                                   | of the relevant changes           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers from Services    |
|                                   | Australia can use SPARC to view   |
|                                   | the historical refurbished status |
|                                   | information as this information   |
|                                   | is not yet available in ACSP      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Manage aged care service      |
|                                   | details for the process           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Refurbished status screen     |
|                                   | displays the following sections:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service banner - displays the     |
|                                   | Service's name, NAPS ID, RACS ID  |
|                                   | (applicable to residential        |
|                                   | services) and Service type        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refurbished status                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refurbished status history -      |
|                                   | displays in a table format:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Reason for update/delete      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | (service) screen                  |

|                                   |     historical declared emergency |
|                                   |     situations for an individual  |
|                                   |     residential care service      |
|                                   | -   is a view only screen         |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | the information in this screen    |

|                                   | ACMPS via the NAPS gateway        |

|                                   |     Epidemic, Pandemic or Other   |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status - the Declared status  |
|                                   |     will display on or before the |
|                                   |     end date of the emergency     |
|                                   |     situation                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Historical emergency situations   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Emergency situation type -    |
|                                   |     displays either Disaster,     |
|                                   |     Epidemic, Pandemic or Other   |
|                                   | -   Care type                     |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status - displays either      |
|                                   |     Ended or Deleted              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword. Search results       |
|                                   |     display where the keyword is  |
|                                   |     used anywhere on the record,  |
|                                   |     even if it appears in the     |
|                                   |     middle of another word        |
