+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Going to and using the View       |
|                                   | manual adjustment screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the View manual adjustment  |
|                                   | screen by:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   selecting the hyperlinked     |
|                                   |     Action status on the Manual   |
|                                   |     adjustment summary screen     |
|                                   | -   the View manual adjustment    |
|                                   |     screen displays the           |
|                                   |     individual record’s details   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the View manual adjustment  |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A manual adjustment is paid to    |
|                                   | the service and can either be     |
|                                   | Positive or Negative              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The reason/purpose for a manual   |
|                                   | adjustment can be classified      |
|                                   | either as a Care recipient        |
|                                   | adjustment or Service adjustment  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For all negative adjustments,     |
|                                   | Service Officers must have        |
|                                   | contacted the service and confirm |
|                                   | if the negative adjustment is to  |
|                                   | be split over a number of months  |
|                                   | (split payments) or included in   |
|                                   | the service’s selected claim      |
|                                   | month                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This must occur before            |
|                                   | registering negative adjustments  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Subject Matter Experts (SME)      |
|                                   | and/or Team Leaders from the Aged |
|                                   | Care Payments Team (Aged Care and |
|                                   | Allied Health Branch) with the    |
|                                   | following roles have the          |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | manual adjustments:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor security role         |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Team Coach Manager  |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View manual adjustment screen |
|                                   | displays the following sections:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View manual adjustment            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   | -   User ID                       |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Document ID                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustment                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Adjustment for                |
|                                   | -   Adjustment payment type       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient adjustment - this  |
|                                   | section will only display if the  |
|                                   | manual adjustment type is Care    |
|                                   | recipient adjustment              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID             |
|                                   | -   Care recipient name           |
|                                   | -   Care recipient allocated      |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   | -   Adjustment type               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Total manual adjustment - this    |
|                                   | section will only display if Care |
|                                   | recipient adjustment has been     |
|                                   | selected for the Adjustment for   |
|                                   | field                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Total manual adjustment       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service adjustment - this section |
|                                   | will only display if the manual   |
|                                   | adjustment type is Service        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Adjustment type               |
|                                   | -   Total manual adjustment       |
|                                   | -   Split over number of months - |
|                                   |     this field will only display  |
|                                   |     if a negative adjustment is   |
|                                   |     being repaid over a number of |
|                                   |     months                        |
|                                   | -   Monthly split amount - this   |
|                                   |     field will only display if a  |
|                                   |     negative adjustment is being  |
|                                   |     repaid over a number of       |
|                                   |     months                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the View manual adjustment   |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can      |
|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Update - go to Step 7         |
|                                   | -   Approve - go to Step 9        |
|                                   | -   Reject - go to Step 9         |
|                                   | -   Close and the Manual          |
|                                   |     adjustment summary screen     |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Going to and using the Register   |
|                                   | manual adjustment screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Register manual      |
|                                   | adjustment screen:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Register manual        |
|                                   |     adjustment on the Manual      |
|                                   |     adjustment summary screen     |
|                                   | -   the Register manual           |
|                                   |     adjustment screen will        |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Register manual         |
|                                   | adjustment screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Register manual        |
|                                   | adjustment screen, Service        |
|                                   | Officers must decide if the       |
|                                   | manual adjustment type in the     |
|                                   | Adjustment for* field is a Care   |
|                                   | recipient adjustment or a Service |
|                                   | adjustment.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Adjustment for* field for  |
|                                   | a care recipient?                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 5             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 6              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Register manual adjustment for a  |
|                                   | care recipient + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Manual adjustments can either |
|                                   |     be Positive or Negative       |
|                                   | -   The Claim month* field can    |
|                                   |     only be the service’s current |
|                                   |     claim month or a future claim |
|                                   |     month. To check the service’s |
|                                   |     current claim month, see Step |
|                                   |     3 of the Using the Aged Care  |
|                                   |     Staff Portal home page table  |
|                                   | -   A split cannot be less than 2 |
|                                   |     months                        |
|                                   | -   This must occur before        |
|                                   |     registering negative          |
|                                   |     adjustments                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can also     |
|                                   |     select Clear to clear the     |
|                                   |     Register manual adjustment    |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register manual adjustment |
|                                   | screen, complete the following:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustment                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim month* field - select   |
|                                   |     the claim month and year from |
|                                   |     the drop down menu            |
|                                   | -   Adjustment for* field -       |
|                                   |     defaults to Please select.    |
|                                   |     Select Care Recipient from    |
|                                   |     the drop down menu            |
|                                   | -   Adjustment payment type*      |
|                                   |     field - select either         |
|                                   |     Positive or Negative          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add care recipient                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID* field -    |
|                                   |     key in the care recipient ID  |
|                                   | -   Care recipient allocated      |
|                                   |     amount* field - key in the    |
|                                   |     adjustment amount             |
|                                   | -   Adjustment type* field -      |
|                                   |     select the relevant reason    |
|                                   |     from the drop down menu. For  |
|                                   |     all negative adjustments,     |
|                                   |     Service Officers must have    |
|                                   |     contacted the service and     |
|                                   |     confirm if the negative       |
|                                   |     adjustment is to be split     |
|                                   |     over a number of months       |
|                                   |     (split payments) or included  |
|                                   |     in the service’s selected     |
|                                   |     claim month                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Add to add more care          |
|                                   |     recipients and repeat the Add |
|                                   |     care recipient process, or    |
|                                   | -   the hyperlinked Remove action |
|                                   |     status to remove a care       |
|                                   |     recipient                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register manual      |
|                                   | adjustment process?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The SUCCESS: Manual           |
|                                   |     adjustment has been created   |
|                                   |     information message will      |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   Select Go to manual           |
|                                   |     adjustments                   |
|                                   | -   The Manual adjustment summary |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   The Cancel? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification displays asking  |
|                                   |     You are about to leave this   |
|                                   |     page, all information will be |
|                                   |     lost. Are you sure you want   |
|                                   |     to cancel?                    |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Manual adjustment summary |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Register manual adjustment for    |
|                                   | the service + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |

|                                   |     be Positive or Negative       |
|                                   | -   A split cannot be less than 2 |
|                                   |     months for the Split over     |
|                                   |     number of months* field       |
|                                   | -   The ‘A split cannot be less   |
|                                   |     than 2 months’ error message  |
|                                   |     will display if Service       |
|                                   |     Officers key either 0 or 1 in |
|                                   |     the Split over number of      |
|                                   |     months* field                 |
|                                   | -   This must occur before        |
|                                   |     registering negative          |
|                                   |     adjustments                   |

|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register manual adjustment |
|                                   | screen, complete the relevant     |
|                                   | fields:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustment                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Claim month* field - select   |
|                                   |     the claim month and year from |
|                                   |     the drop down menu            |
|                                   | -   Adjustment for* field -       |
|                                   |     defaults to Please select.    |
|                                   |     Select Service from the drop  |
|                                   |     down menu                     |
|                                   | -   Adjustment payment type*      |
|                                   |     field - select either         |
|                                   |     Positive or Negative. For all |

|                                   |     Officers must have contacted  |
|                                   |     the service and confirm if    |
|                                   |     the negative adjustment is to |
|                                   |     be split over a number of     |
|                                   |     months (split payments) or    |
|                                   |     included in the service’s     |
|                                   |     selected claim month          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service adjustment                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Adjustment type* field -      |
|                                   |     defaults to Please select.    |
|                                   |     Select the relevant reason    |
|                                   |     from the drop down menu       |
|                                   | -   Total manual adjustment*      |
|                                   |     field - key in the adjustment |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   | -   Split payment* - select       |
|                                   |     either Yes or No              |
|                                   | -   Split over number of months*  |
|                                   |     field - displays if Yes has   |
|                                   |     been selected for Split       |
|                                   |     payment*                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register manual      |
|                                   | adjustment process?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   The Cancel? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification displays asking  |
|                                   |     You are about to leave this   |
|                                   |     page, all information will be |
|                                   |     lost. Are you sure you want   |
|                                   |     to cancel?                    |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Manual adjustment summary |

| 7                                 | Going to and using the Update     |
|                                   | manual adjustment screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Manual adjustments with       |
|                                   |     either the Created or Updated |
|                                   |     status can only be updated    |
|                                   | -   Service Officers are unable   |
|                                   |     to update both the Adjustment |
|                                   |     for* and Adjustment payment   |
|                                   |     type* fields                  |
|                                   | -   If either the Adjustment for* |
|                                   |     or Adjustment payment type*   |
|                                   |     field is incorrect, Service   |
|                                   |     Officers must have the manual |
|                                   |     adjustment rejected and       |
|                                   |     create (register) a new       |
|                                   |     manual adjustment             |
|                                   | -   A split cannot be less than 2 |
|                                   |     months for the Split over     |
|                                   |     number of months* field       |
|                                   | -   The A split cannot be less    |
|                                   |     than 2 months error message   |
|                                   |     will display if Service       |
|                                   |     Officers key either 0 or 1 in |
|                                   |     the Split over number of      |
|                                   |     months* field                 |

|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Update manual        |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add care recipient - this section |
|                                   | will only display if the manual   |
|                                   | adjustment type is Care recipient |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     key in any additional care    |
|                                   |     recipients and select Add     |
|                                   | -   Care recipient allocated      |
|                                   |     amount* field - key in the    |
|                                   |     updated adjustment amount     |
|                                   | -   Adjustment type* field -      |
|                                   |     select the relevant reason    |
|                                   |     from the drop down menu       |

|                                   | -   Adjustment type* field -      |
|                                   |     select the relevant reason    |
|                                   |     from the drop down menu       |
|                                   | -   Total manual adjustment*      |
|                                   |     field - key in the updated    |
|                                   |     adjustment amount             |
|                                   | -   Split over number of months*  |
|                                   |     field - displays if Yes has   |
|                                   |     been selected for Split       |
|                                   |     payment*                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |

| 8                                 | Viewing the Receipt screen + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: The Receipt screen displays |
|                                   | when a manual adjustment has      |
|                                   | either been created or updated.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the successful receipt            |
|                                   | information message               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the summary of who created or     |
|                                   | updated the manual adjustment     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   | -   Submission date               |
|                                   | -   Submitted by                  |
|                                   | -   Claim month                   |
|                                   | -   Total adjustment amount       |
|                                   | -   Split over number of months - |
|                                   |     displays if Yes has been      |
|                                   |     selected for Split payment*   |
|                                   | -   Split amount - displays if    |
|                                   |     Yes has been selected for     |
|                                   |     Split payment*                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must select Go   |
|                                   | to manual adjustments and the     |
|                                   | Manual adjustment summary screen  |
|                                   | will display.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Approve or reject manual          |
|                                   | adjustment + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SME and/or Team Leaders from the  |
|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |
|                                   | with the following roles have the |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | manual adjustments:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor security role         |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Team Coach Manager  |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustments with the       |
|                                   | Created or Updated status can     |
|                                   | only either be approved, updated  |
|                                   | or rejected                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A different user to the one who   |
|                                   | created or updated the manual     |
|                                   | advance at any point can approve  |
|                                   | or reject the manual advance      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustments with the       |
|                                   | Approved status can be rejected   |
|                                   | if the manual adjustment’s linked |
|                                   | Claim month has not been          |
|                                   | finalised                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Approve:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Approve on the View manual |
|                                   | adjustment screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Approve? pop up notification  |
|                                   | will display                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘SUCCESS: The manual          |
|                                   | adjustment has been successfully  |
|                                   | approved’ information message     |
|                                   | will display                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Close to return to the     |
|                                   | Manual adjustment summary screen  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Add service note detailing the    |
|                                   | manual adjustment                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See the Using the Aged Care   |
|                                   |     Staff Portal to manage        |
|                                   |     residential care service      |
|                                   |     notes table                   |
|                                   | -   Use the following format:     |
|                                   |     <Manual adjustment            |
|                                   |     type>$##.##                   |
|                                   | -   An example is Positive manual |
|                                   |     adjustment $123.45            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Reject a manual advance:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Reject on the View     |
|                                   |     manual adjustment screen      |
|                                   | -   The Reject? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification will display     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Manual adjustment summary |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   The rejected manual           |
|                                   |     adjustment will display in    |
|                                   |     the Historical manual         |
|                                   |     adjustments section           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

|                                   | -   the Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Using the Care recipient search   |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers may need to  |
|                                   |     refine their search results   |
|                                   |     if the 'Your search matched X |
|                                   |     care recipients. Only 200     |
|                                   |     care recipients are displayed |
|                                   |     in care recipient ID order    |
|                                   |     below. Please refine your     |
|                                   |     search criteria if needed'    |
|                                   |     information message displays  |
|                                   |     and they cannot locate the    |
|                                   |     relevant care recipient from  |
|                                   |     the search results            |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use the Care recipient search     |
|                                   | screen to search for a care       |
|                                   | recipient by:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient details        |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Getaway (ACG) ID    |
|                                   | -   Centrelink ID                 |
|                                   | -   Department of Veterans’       |
|                                   |     Affairs (DVA) ID              |
|                                   | -   Recent searches               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Care recipient       |
|                                   | details + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Care recipient details in  |
|                                   | the Search by* field              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | complete the below fields         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care recipient ID* Note: if   |
|                                   |     searching by Care recipient   |
|                                   |     ID, the mandatory asterisk    |
|                                   |     against the Family name field |
|                                   |     disappears                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Given name                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Family name* Note: the        |
|                                   |     spelling must be the exact    |
|                                   |     Care recipient's family name. |
|                                   |     If searching by Family name,  |
|                                   |     the mandatory asterisk        |
|                                   |     against the Care recipient ID |
|                                   |     field disappears.             |
|                                   | -   Date of birth                 |
|                                   | -   Gender - select from the drop |
|                                   |     down list                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Search button      |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Aged Care Getaway    |
|                                   | (ACG) ID + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Aged Care Getaway      |
|                                   |     (ACG) ID in the Search by*    |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   | -   key the Aged Care Getaway     |
|                                   |     (ACG) ID in the ACG ID* field |
|                                   | -   select the Search button      |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Centrelink ID + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Centrelink ID in the   |
|                                   |     Search by* field              |
|                                   | -   key the Centrelink ID in the  |
|                                   |     Centrelink ID* field          |
|                                   | -   select the Search button      |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Department of        |
|                                   | Veterans’ Affairs (DVA) ID + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Department of          |
|                                   |     Veterans’ Affairs (DVA) ID in |
|                                   |     the Search by* field          |
|                                   | -   key the DVA ID in the DVA     |
|                                   |     ID * field                    |
|                                   | -   select the Search button      |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Search by Recent searches +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Care recipient ID |

|                                   |     section results table         |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 12                                | Using the Care recipients’        |
|                                   | details screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the column headings in the  |
|                                   | Care recipients' details screen   |
|                                   | are frozen and visible for        |

|                                   | details.                          |

|                                   | screen displays the following     |

|                                   | -   Reappraisal dates -           |
|                                   |     Mandatory, Optional, Worker’s |
|                                   |     compensation (WC)/Third Party |
|                                   |     (TP) and room type            |
|                                   | -   Leave days left - displays    |
|                                   |     the Respite Care (RC) and     |
|                                   |     Transition Care (TC) balances |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Care recipients’ details   |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can:     |

|                                   | for a care recipient by care      |
|                                   | recipient ID or care recipient    |
|                                   | name                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To view specific details of a |

|                                   |     recipient ID hyperlink. Note: |
|                                   |     Service Officers can search   |
|                                   |     for a care recipient via a    |
|                                   |     partial search                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant Claim month   |
|                                   | from the drop down list           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | view the RC and TC leave balances |
|                                   | for care recipients               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records from |
|                                   | the Show records drop down list   |
|                                   | (bottom left hand corner of the   |
|                                   | screen)                           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the relevant format option |
|                                   | to download the payment summary   |
|                                   | in CSV, XML or PDF format         |

| 13                                | Viewing an individual care        |
|                                   | recipient’s profile details +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | ID to display the individual care |
|                                   | recipient profile.                |

|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient tab                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Approval details - this       |
|                                   |     includes current and          |
|                                   |     historical approval details   |
|                                   | -   Event summary. Select the     |
|                                   |     Register button under the     |
|                                   |     relevant event type to        |

|                                   |     display individual event's    |
|                                   |     details                       |

|                                   | this tab is only applicable to    |

|                                   | select the ACFI summary to        |
|                                   | display the current and           |
|                                   | historical ACFI details           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | relevant event type to view       |
|                                   | details. Select the Register      |
|                                   | button under the relevant event   |
|                                   | type to register new events or    |
|                                   | select the hyperlinked Status ID  |
|                                   | to display individual event's     |
|                                   | details                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Supplements tab - this tab is     |
|                                   | only applicable to home and       |
|                                   | residential care services. Select |
|                                   | the relevant supplement type to   |
|                                   | view details. Select the Register |
|                                   | button under the relevant         |
|                                   | supplement type to register new   |
|                                   | supplement or select the          |
|                                   | hyperlinked Status ID to display  |
|                                   | the individual supplement’s       |
|                                   | details                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional days - this tab is     |
|                                   | only applicable to transition     |
|                                   | care services. Select the tab to  |
|                                   | view additional transition care   |
|                                   | days’ information                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Commonwealth amount tab - this    |
|                                   | tab is only applicable to home    |
|                                   | care services. Select the tab to  |
|                                   | display CW Unspent amounts -      |
|                                   | Report and opt in, CW Unspent     |
|                                   | amount on departure, Invoice      |
|                                   | amount and Home care account. Go  |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: Service Officers can select |
|                                   | Home to return to the ACSP        |
|                                   | Service in Context home page      |

|                                   |     in context’s current claim is |

|                                   |     onwards                       |
|                                   | -   displays the details of an    |
|                                   |     individual reported           |
|                                   |     Commonwealth (CW) unspent     |
|                                   |     amount                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Update reported        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | complete the following fields:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Amount*                       |
|                                   | -   Opt in - only available       |
|                                   |     during the opt-in period      |
|                                   |     (that is, 1 September 2021 to |
|                                   |     28 February 2022 inclusive)   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select either                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Submit to complete the Update |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount process                |
|                                   | -   Cancel and return to the View |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Delete a Reported Commonwealth |
|                                   | unspent amount                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select in the Delete? pop up      |
|                                   | notification either:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes to complete the deletion  |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Cancel and return to the View |
|                                   |     reported Commonwealth unspent |
|                                   |     amount screen                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   | -   select the hyperlinked        |
|                                   |     Service NAPS ID in the search |
|                                   |     results table                 |
|                                   | -   the ACSP Service in Context   |
|                                   |     home page displays            |
|                                   | -   select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) under the Service   |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     (service) screen displays     |
|                                   | -   key the care recipient’s      |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   select Search                 |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient service    |
|                                   |     entries screen displays       |
|                                   | -   select Go to current profile  |
|                                   | -   the Care recipient profile    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |

|                                   |     amount tab                    |
|                                   | -   hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth amount menu  |
|                                   |     tab                           |
|                                   | -   a pop up window displays      |
|                                   | -   select CW Unspent amount on   |
|                                   |     departure                     |

|                                   |                                   |

| 10                                | Registering Bulk reporting        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Bulk reporting            |
|                                   |     Commonwealth unspent amounts  |
|                                   |     screen is available when the  |
|                                   |     service in context’s current  |
|                                   |     claim is the September 2021   |
|                                   |     claim onwards                 |
|                                   | -   An error message will display |
|                                   |     if the Amount* field has not  |
|                                   |     been completed for all care   |
|                                   |     recipients. Service Officers  |
|                                   |     must either enter the missing |
|                                   |     amounts or set all the care   |
|                                   |     recipients’ Amount* field to  |
|                                   |     zero dollars ($0) by          |
|                                   |     selecting Set to 0.0          |
|                                   | -   If the event has been         |
|                                   |     submitted successfully, a     |
|                                   |     successful receipt message    |
|                                   |     will display                  |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must carefully   |
|                                   | review each care recipient’s      |
|                                   | information before submitting the |
|                                   | Bulk reporting Commonwealth       |
|                                   | unspent amounts events.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Bulk reporting Commonwealth   |
|                                   | unspent amounts screen displays   |
|                                   | the following information in a    |
|                                   | table format:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care recipient                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ID                            |
|                                   | -   Given name                    |
|                                   | -   Family name                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amount       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Amount                        |
|                                   | -   Opt in - only available       |
|                                   |     during the opt-in period      |
|                                   |     (that is, 1 September 2021 to |
|                                   |     28 February 2022 inclusive)   |
|                                   | -   Submission Status             |
|                                   | -   Event Status                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To register Bulk reporting        |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts,     |
|                                   | complete:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Amount* field             |
|                                   | -   the Opt in field - only       |
|                                   |     available during the opt-in   |
|                                   |     period (that is, 1 September  |
|                                   |     2021 to 28 February 2022      |
|                                   |     inclusive)                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete registering the Bulk     |
|                                   | reporting Commonwealth unspent    |
|                                   | amounts process?                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Bulk reporting Commonwealth   |
|                                   |     unspent amounts process       |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type in a keyword in the Search   |
|                                   | bar to search for all records     |
|                                   | that contain the keyword          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | filter the records by the         |
|                                   | Submission Status to narrow the   |
|                                   | records                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Delete All to delete all   |
|                                   | Bulk reporting Commonwealth       |
|                                   | unspent amounts records           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Import CSV to perform a    |
|                                   | bulk import of Bulk reporting     |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts from |
|                                   | a CSV file                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Export CSV to export all   |
|                                   | the content of the Bulk reporting |
|                                   | Commonwealth unspent amounts      |
|                                   | screen into a CSV file            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | set all the care recipients’      |
|                                   | Amount* field to zero dollars     |
|                                   | ($0) by selecting Set to 0.0      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Check all submitted Opt in |
|                                   | to opt in all care recipients for |
|                                   | the current claim month           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the number of records to   |
|                                   | display from the Show records     |
|                                   | drop down list (bottom left       |
|                                   | corner of the screen)             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Go to the current claim to |
|                                   | display the Current claim screen  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Close to return to the     |
|                                   | ACSP Service in Context home page |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | go to a different page by         |
|                                   | selecting either the:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   First, Previous, Next or Last |
|                                   |     options, or                   |
|                                   | -   the relevant page number      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Delete? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification will display     |
|                                   |     asking Service Officers to    |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the event                     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes and the individual |
|                                   |     Invoice amount entry is       |
|                                   |     deleted                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 15                                | The Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   displays for home care        |
|                                   |     services only                 |
|                                   | -   is available when the service |
|                                   |     in context’s current claim is |
|                                   |     the September 2021 claim      |
|                                   |     onwards                       |
|                                   | -   displays Care Recipient       |
|                                   |     banner - displays the care    |
|                                   |     recipient’s name, IDs, Date   |
|                                   |     of Birth, Record type and     |
|                                   |     Type of care status           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Claim month field defaults to |
|                                   | the service the service in        |
|                                   | context’s current claim month     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Invoice amounts cannot be updated |
|                                   | once the claim has been           |
|                                   | finalised. If a previous invoice  |
|                                   | amount has been incorrectly       |
|                                   | entered, Service Officers can use |
|                                   | the Register invoice amount       |
|                                   | screen to reflect the adjustment. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 1          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount was originally $60,000 |
|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in June 2023 that  |
|                                   |     the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount should have been       |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   the June 2023 invoice amount  |
|                                   |     has been calculated as        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can use the  |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     screen to add the additional  |
|                                   |     $40,000 as part of the        |
|                                   |     current claim month’s invoice |
|                                   |     amount by entering an invoice |
|                                   |     amount of $140,000 for June   |
|                                   |     2023                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 2          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the March 2023 invoice amount |
|                                   |     was originally $140,000       |
|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in July 2023 that  |
|                                   |     the March 2023 invoice amount |
|                                   |     should have been $100,000     |
|                                   | -   the July 2023 invoice amount  |
|                                   |     has been calculated as        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can use the  |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     screen to reduce the current  |
|                                   |     claim month’s invoice amount  |
|                                   |     by $40,000 by entering an     |
|                                   |     invoice amount of $60,000 for |
|                                   |     July 2023                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Register invoice amount,       |
|                                   | complete the Amount* field.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete registering the Register |
|                                   | invoice amount?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Register invoice amount       |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 16                                | The Update invoice amount         |

|                                   | Note:                             |

|                                   | Invoice amounts cannot be updated |
|                                   | once the claim has been           |
|                                   | finalised. If a previous invoice  |
|                                   | amount has been incorrectly       |
|                                   | entered, Service Officers can use |
|                                   | the Update invoice amount screen  |
|                                   | for the current claim month to    |
|                                   | reflect the adjustment.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 1          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount was originally $60,000 |
|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in June 2023 that  |
|                                   |     the December 2022 invoice     |
|                                   |     amount should had been        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   the June 2023 invoice amount  |
|                                   |     has been calculated as        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
