|                                   |     Update invoice amount screen  |
|                                   |     to add the additional $40,000 |
|                                   |     as part of the current claim  |
|                                   |     month’s invoice amount. That  |
|                                   |     is, update June 2023’s        |

|                                   |     to $140,000                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For example - scenario 2          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   the home care service         |
|                                   |     determined in August 2023     |
|                                   |     that the March 2023 invoice   |
|                                   |     amount should had been        |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   the August 2023 invoice       |
|                                   |     amount has been calculated as |
|                                   |     $100,000                      |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can use the  |
|                                   |     Update invoice amount screen  |
|                                   |     to reduce the current claim   |
|                                   |     month’s invoice amount by     |
|                                   |     $40,000. That is, update      |
|                                   |     August 2023’s invoice amount  |
|                                   |     from $100,000 to $60,000      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Update invoice amount, make    |
|                                   | the updates in the Amount* field. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete registering the Update   |
|                                   | invoice amount?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful recipient      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel to cancel the   |
|                                   |     Update invoice amount process |
|                                   | -   The Cancel message will       |
|                                   |     display asking Service        |
|                                   |     Officers to select Yes or No  |
|                                   |     to cancel the event           |

Registering events in the Aged Care Staff Portal (Service in Context)

Table 15

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Register an event in the Aged     |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal (ACSP) + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the ACSP:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Register an entry event - go  |
|                                   |     to Step 2                     |
|                                   | -   Register a leave event - go   |
|                                   |     to Step 7                     |
|                                   | -   Register a departure event -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 8                  |
|                                   | -   Register care setting days -  |
|                                   |     go to Step 10                 |
|                                   | -   Register bulk events - go to  |
|                                   |     Step 12                       |
|                                   | -   Update an existing event - go |
|                                   |     to Step 15                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Register an entry event + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   For residential care entry    |
|                                   |     events, see Table 16 - Using  |
|                                   |     the Aged Care Staff Portal to |
|                                   |     register residential entry    |
|                                   |     events - (Service in Context) |
|                                   | -   The entry date must be within |
|                                   |     the last 2 years of the       |
|                                   |     current date                  |
|                                   | -   This step is applicable to    |
|                                   |     all care types except         |
|                                   |     residential care              |
|                                   | -   All fields are mandatory      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events are registered in an |
|                                   | individual care recipient         |
|                                   | profile:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Entry summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Register entry button  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Register entry screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register entry screen,     |
|                                   | complete:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Type of care* field               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the relevant care type |
|                                   |     from the drop-down field      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Hospital admission date* field -  |
|                                   | this is only applicable for       |
|                                   | transition care recipients        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry date* field                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Level of care* field - applicable |
|                                   | for home care recipients only     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Carer status* field - applicable  |
|                                   | for home care recipients only     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Functional capacity score (MBI)   |
|                                   | on entry* field - applicable for  |
|                                   | flexible care recipients only     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Register entry event       |
|                                   | process complete?                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 3                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the process                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Check the entry event’s status +  |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An entry event is successful when |
|                                   | the status is Accepted.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the entry event successful?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The entry event status is a   |
|                                   |     Held status                   |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 4                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Review held entry events + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Entry events with a Held status   |
|                                   | will not be processed as part of  |
|                                   | the current claim’s finalisation  |
|                                   | process which may result in over  |
|                                   | occupancy issues.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Held entry events are due to      |
|                                   | either a:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   known timing issue with over  |
|                                   |     lapping periods of care, or   |
|                                   | -   genuine over lapping period   |
|                                   |     of care                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A known timing issue with         |
|                                   | overlapping periods of care is    |
|                                   | where the care recipient has      |
|                                   | entered in to care of the new     |
|                                   | aged care service but a departure |
|                                   | event has not been submitted by   |
|                                   | the previous aged care service.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | These entry events are resolved   |
|                                   | when Services Australia has       |
|                                   | received the departure event from |
|                                   | the previous aged care service.   |
|                                   | No manual intervention is         |
|                                   | required from Service Officers.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the held entry event due to a  |
|                                   | known timing issue?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   No manual intervention is     |
|                                   |     required from Service         |
|                                   |     Officers                      |
|                                   | -   The entry event will be       |
|                                   |     resolved when Services        |
|                                   |     Australia has received the    |
|                                   |     departure event from the      |
|                                   |     previous aged care service    |
|                                   | -   Process is complete           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 5                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Remediate genuine overlapping     |
|                                   | entry and departure dates between |
|                                   | 2 services + Read more ...        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A genuine overlapping period of   |
|                                   | care is where the care recipient  |
|                                   | has entered into care of the new  |
|                                   | aged care service and the entry   |
|                                   | event overlaps with the departure |
|                                   | event submitted by the previous   |
|                                   | aged care service.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For held entry events due to a    |
|                                   | genuine overlapping period of     |
|                                   | care, manually remediate these    |
|                                   | cases to ensure the entry event   |
|                                   | is accepted.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To remediate the overlap:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   identify the ‘source’ service |
|                                   |     (that is, identify the        |
|                                   |     service the care recipient    |
|                                   |     would have been entered into  |
|                                   |     first)                        |
|                                   | -   map out the entry and         |
|                                   |     departure dates for each      |
|                                   |     service and put them into the |
|                                   |     correct date order            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Contact the service to confirm    |
|                                   | the correct entry or departure    |
|                                   | date.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have the correct entry or         |
|                                   | departure dates been confirmed?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Update the events’ dates to   |
|                                   |     ‘remove the overlap’ in dates |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 14 for the process |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Do not process the entry or   |
|                                   |     departure events              |
|                                   | -   Create a care recipient note  |
|                                   |     advising an attempt to        |
|                                   |     contact the service was       |
|                                   |     unsuccessful and no action    |
|                                   |     has been taken. See Step 4 in |
|                                   |     the Using the Aged Care Staff |
|                                   |     Portal to manage care         |
|                                   |     recipient notes table         |
|                                   | -   Create a payment statement    |
|                                   |     note in ACMPS, see Step 2 in  |
|                                   |     the Maintain payment          |
|                                   |     statements notes in ACMPS     |
|                                   |     table. Use suggested wording  |
|                                   |     “[CR number and name] unable  |
|                                   |     to process entry/departure    |
|                                   |     due to overlap in dates with  |
|                                   |     another service. Please       |
|                                   |     reclaim.”                     |
|                                   | -   Re-finalise the claim. See    |
|                                   |     Step 5 in Table 2 for the     |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Add a care recipient note for     |
|                                   | successful contacts and           |
|                                   | re-finalise the claim + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When the updates to the events’   |
|                                   | dates have been completed:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a care recipient note. The |
|                                   | care recipient note must include  |
|                                   | the full name and contact number  |
|                                   | of service contact the Service    |
|                                   | Officer had spoken to and         |
|                                   | confirmation of action undertaken |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Step 4 in the Using the   |
|                                   |     Aged Care Staff Portal to     |
|                                   |     manage care recipient notes   |
|                                   |     table                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | re-finalise the claim             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Step 5 in Table 2 for the |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Register a leave event + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For flexible care services select |
|                                   | a start date less than 2 years    |
|                                   | before (or equal to) the current  |
|                                   | date                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For residential care services     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers with either  |
|                                   |     the Aged Care Service Officer |
|                                   |     or Aged Care Fees and Charges |
|                                   |     security role must select a   |
|                                   |     start date less than 2 years  |
|                                   |     before (or equal to) the      |
|                                   |     current date                  |
|                                   | -   An error message will display |
|                                   |     to these Service Officers if  |
|                                   |     the start date is beyond the  |
|                                   |     2 year limit                  |
|                                   | -   Service Officers with either  |
|                                   |     the Aged Care Technical       |
|                                   |     Program Advisor or Business   |
|                                   |     Administrator security role   |
|                                   |     can select a start date       |
|                                   |     beyond the 2 year limit       |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must be      |
|                                   |     satisfied with the request    |
|                                   |     and relevant supporting       |
|                                   |     evidence from the aged care   |
|                                   |     service prior to registering  |
|                                   |     events beyond the 2 year      |
|                                   |     limit                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care leave events that   |
|                                   | occurred on or after 1 September  |
|                                   | 2021 onwards, select a date that  |
|                                   | is less than:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   2 years before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who are still in   |
|                                   |     the service’s care            |
|                                   | -   70 days before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who have departed  |
|                                   |     from the service              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care leave events that   |
|                                   | occurred prior to 1 September     |
|                                   | 2021:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select a date that is less    |
|                                   |     than 2 years before (or equal |
|                                   |     to) the current date          |
|                                   | -   this applies for all current  |
|                                   |     and departed care recipients  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event submits              |
|                                   | successfully, a successful        |
|                                   | message displays                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register a leave event in an      |
|                                   | individual care recipient         |
|                                   | profile:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select Leave                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Leave summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select the Register leave button  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Register leave screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | select an option from the Leave   |
|                                   | type* drop down list              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type the start date in the Leave  |
|                                   | start date* field                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | type the end date in the Leave    |
|                                   | end date field                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Register leave event       |
|                                   | complete?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, select Submit                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the event                     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Register leave event      |
|                                   |     process has been cancelled    |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

| 14                                | Updating an existing event + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |

|                                   | -   Service Officers with either  |

|                                   |     or Aged Care Fees and Charges |
|                                   |     security role must select a   |
|                                   |     start date less than 2 years  |
|                                   |     before (or equal to) the      |
|                                   |     current date                  |
|                                   | -   An error message will display |
|                                   |     to these Service Officers if  |
|                                   |     the start date is beyond the  |
|                                   |     2 year limit                  |
|                                   | -   Service Officers with either  |
|                                   |     the Aged Care Technical       |
|                                   |     Program Advisor or Business   |
|                                   |     Administrator security role   |
|                                   |     can select a start date       |
|                                   |     beyond the 2 year limit       |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must be      |
|                                   |     satisfied with the request    |
|                                   |     and relevant supporting       |
|                                   |     evidence from the aged care   |
|                                   |     service prior to updating     |
|                                   |     events beyond the 2 year      |
|                                   |     limit                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care events that         |
|                                   | occurred on or after 1 September  |
|                                   | 2021 onwards, select a date that  |
|                                   | is less than:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   2 years before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who are still in   |
|                                   |     the service’s care            |
|                                   | -   70 days before (or equal to)  |
|                                   |     the current date for care     |
|                                   |     recipients who have departed  |
|                                   |     from the service’s care       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For home care events that         |
|                                   | occurred prior to 1 September     |
|                                   | 2021:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select a date that is less    |
|                                   |     than 2 years before (or equal |
|                                   |     to) the current date          |
|                                   | -   this applies for all current  |
|                                   |     and departed care recipients  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event submits              |
|                                   | successfully, a successful        |
|                                   | message displays                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update or delete an event in the  |
|                                   | individual event’s details screen |
|                                   | (the event history):              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the Update button and  |
|                                   |     add the relevant details, or  |
|                                   | -   select the Delete button      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the update (or deletion)       |
|                                   | complete?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Submit to complete the |
|                                   |     process                       |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel                 |
|                                   | -   A message displays asking to  |
|                                   |     select Yes or No to cancel    |
|                                   |     the update (or deletion)      |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The update (or deletion) has  |
|                                   |     been cancelled                |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

| 6                                 | Register permanent residential    |

|                                   |     the Commonwealth or an agent  |
|                                   |     of the Commonwealth or        |

|                                   |     taken                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Submit                     |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to approve, delete, reject or update residential entry events - (Service in Context)

Table 17

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Choose Menu options in ACSP +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: see                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Table 16 for the process of       |
|                                   | registering residential entry     |
|                                   | events.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use this process table:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   to approve, delete, reject or |
|                                   |     update residential entry      |
|                                   |     events                        |
|                                   | -   applies to permanent and      |
|                                   |     respite residential entry     |
|                                   |     events                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP service in context  |
|                                   | home page, Service Officers must  |
|                                   | go to a care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   | to do this. See Table 12, Step 2  |
|                                   | for the process of Going to the   |
|                                   | Care recipient search screen.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | option:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Approve permanent residential |
|                                   |     entry events - go to Step 2   |
|                                   | -   Delete permanent residential  |
|                                   |     entry events - go to Step 3   |
|                                   | -   Reject permanent residential  |
|                                   |     entry events - go to Step 4   |
|                                   | -   Update permanent residential  |
|                                   |     entry events - go to Step 5   |
|                                   | -   Update or delete respite      |
|                                   |     residential entry events - go |
|                                   |     to Step 6                     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Approve permanent residential     |
|                                   | entry events + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Held permanent residential entry  |
|                                   | events can only be approved after |
|                                   | the New Aged Care Arrangements    |
|                                   | from 1 July 2014 (AC022) form has |
|                                   | been assessed for completion      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See the Checking and          |
|                                   |     assessing the AC022 form is   |
|                                   |     complete table for more       |
|                                   |     information                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Subject Matter Experts (SME)      |
|                                   | and/or Team Leaders from the Aged |
|                                   | Care Payments Team (Aged Care and |
|                                   | Allied Health Branch) with either |
|                                   | the Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   | Advisor or Business Administrator |
|                                   | security role have the authority  |
|                                   | to approve held permanent         |
|                                   | residential entry events          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SME and/or Team Leaders can also  |
|                                   | select Back to display the        |
|                                   | previous View entry screen        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Approve permanent residential  |
|                                   | entry events with Held status:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entry summary screen displays |
|                                   | the following table               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View entry screen will        |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next until the View        |
|                                   | entry - Step 4 screen displays    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Approve on the View        |
|                                   | entry - Step 4 screen             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Approve? pop up notification  |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the SME and/or Team Leaders  |
|                                   | want to complete the Approval     |
|                                   | process?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The entry event’s status in   |
|                                   |     the Entry summary screen will |
|                                   |     change from Held to Accepted  |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select No                     |
|                                   | -   The View entry - Step 4       |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Delete permanent residential      |
|                                   | entry events + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can also     |

|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |

|                                   | Status                            |

|                                   | Select Delete                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Delete? pop up notification   |
|                                   | will display                      |

|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   The entry event’s status in   |
|                                   |     the Entry summary screen will |
|                                   |     display as Deleted            |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must Add     |
|                                   |     care recipient notes of Using |
|                                   |     the Aged Care Staff Portal to |
|                                   |     manage care recipient notes   |
|                                   |     (Care Recipient in Context    |
|                                   |     (CRiC))                       |
|                                   | -   Document clear and accurate   |
|                                   |     notes detailing the action    |
|                                   |     taken                         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel and return to   |
|                                   |     the View entry screen         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |

| 4                                 | Reject permanent residential      |
|                                   | entry events + Read more ...      |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |

|                                   | Technical Program Advisor or      |
|                                   | Business Administrator security   |

|                                   | the following table               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View entry screen will        |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Next until the View        |
|                                   | entry - Step 4 screen displays    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Reject on the View entry - |
|                                   | Step 4 screen                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Reject? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |

|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | want to complete the Reject Held  |
|                                   | permanent residential entry       |
|                                   | events process?                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document clear and accurate   |
|                                   |     notes detailing the action    |
|                                   |     taken in the Reject? pop up   |
|                                   |     notification                  |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The entry event’s status in   |
|                                   |     the Entry summary screen will |
|                                   |     change from Held to Rejected  |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select No                     |
|                                   | -   The View entry - Step 4       |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Update permanent residential      |
|                                   | entry events + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff with either the Aged Care   |
|                                   | Technical Program Advisor or      |
|                                   | Business Administrator security   |
|                                   | role can update events older than |
|                                   | 2 years before (or equal to) the  |
|                                   | current date                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | They can only do this if all of   |
|                                   | the following conditions have     |
|                                   | been satisfied:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the aged care service has     |
|                                   |     provided supporting evidence  |
|                                   |     with the request to change    |
|                                   |     (vary) an event outside the 2 |
|                                   |     year limit and                |
|                                   | -   they are satisfied with the   |
|                                   |     request to change (vary) an   |
|                                   |     event outside the 2 year      |
|                                   |     limit event and               |
|                                   | -   the request to (vary) an      |
|                                   |     event is a result of an       |
|                                   |     administrative error made by  |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth or an agent  |
|                                   |     of the Commonwealth or        |
|                                   | -   the request to (vary) an      |
|                                   |     event is a result of          |
|                                   |     determining the circumstances |
|                                   |     of a care recipient are       |
|                                   |     different from those on the   |
|                                   |     basis the subsidy was claimed |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An error message will display to  |
|                                   | staff who do not have the correct |
|                                   | access permission when updating   |
|                                   | events outside the 2 year limit   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff can key the date            |
|                                   | (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from the  |
|                                   | calendar (select the calendar     |
|                                   | icon to display the calendar)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff can also select either      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Cancel to cancel the Update   |
|                                   |     entry process                 |
|                                   | -   Back to display the previous  |
|                                   |     Update entry screen           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Update permanent residential   |
|                                   | entry events:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entry summary screen displays |
|                                   | the following table               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View entry screen will        |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Update                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make the changes to the relevant  |
|                                   | Update entry screen               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the staff want to complete   |
|                                   | the Update permanent residential  |
|                                   | entry events process?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Next until the Update  |
|                                   |     entry - Step 4 screen         |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   | -   Document clear and accurate   |
|                                   |     notes detailing the action    |
|                                   |     taken in the Entry notes (500 |
|                                   |     character limit) field        |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The SUCCESS: Permanent        |
|                                   |     residential care entry has    |
|                                   |     been updated information      |
|                                   |     message will display          |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select No                     |
|                                   | -   The View entry - Step 4       |
|                                   |     screen will display           |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Update or delete respite          |
|                                   | residential entry events + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Is the care recipient in an   |
|                                   | extra service place? field in the |
|                                   | Extra service details section is  |
|                                   | greyed out where the residential  |
|                                   | care service does not have extra  |
|                                   | service places                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff with either the Aged Care   |
|                                   | Technical Program Advisor or      |
|                                   | Business Administrator security   |
|                                   | role can update events older than |
|                                   | 2 years before (or equal to) the  |
|                                   | current date                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | They can only do this if all of   |
|                                   | the following conditions have     |
|                                   | been satisfied:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the aged care service has     |
|                                   |     provided supporting evidence  |
|                                   |     with the request to change    |
|                                   |     (vary) an event outside the 2 |
|                                   |     year limit and                |
|                                   | -   they are satisfied with the   |
|                                   |     request to change (vary) an   |
|                                   |     event outside the 2 year      |
|                                   |     limit event and               |
|                                   | -   the request to (vary) an      |
|                                   |     event is a result of an       |
|                                   |     administrative error made by  |
|                                   |     the Commonwealth or an agent  |
|                                   |     of the Commonwealth, or       |
|                                   | -   the request to (vary) an      |
|                                   |     event is a result of          |
|                                   |     determining the circumstances |
|                                   |     of a care recipient are       |
|                                   |     different from those on the   |
|                                   |     basis the subsidy was claimed |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An error message will display to  |
|                                   | staff who do not have the correct |
|                                   | access permission when updating   |
|                                   | events outside the 2 year limit   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff can key the date            |
|                                   | (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from the  |
|                                   | calendar (select the calendar     |
|                                   | icon to display the calendar)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All updates or deletion to        |
|                                   | respite residential entry events  |
|                                   | are done in an individual care    |
|                                   | recipient profile (Service in     |
|                                   | Context).                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Deletion of respite residential   |
|                                   | entry events has impacts for both |
|                                   | care recipients and the aged care |
|                                   | service. If the aged care service |
|                                   | has requested the deletion and    |
|                                   | has not provided reasons for the  |
|                                   | deletion, staff can contact the   |
|                                   | aged care service for further     |
|                                   | information.                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Update respite residential     |
|                                   | entry:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entry summary screen displays |
|                                   | the following table               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View entry screen will        |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Update                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make the relevant updates to the  |
|                                   | following fields if applicable    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type of care                  |
|                                   | -   Entry details                 |
|                                   | -   Adjusted subsidy indicator    |
|                                   | -   Compensation details          |
|                                   | -   Extra service details         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Submit                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The SUCCESS: Respite residential  |
|                                   | care entry has been updated       |
|                                   | information message will display  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff must Add care recipient     |
|                                   | notes of Using the Aged Care      |
|                                   | Staff Portal to manage care       |
|                                   | recipient notes (Care Recipient   |
|                                   | in Context (CRiC))                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document clear and accurate notes |
|                                   | detailing the action taken        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Delete respite residential     |
|                                   | entry:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Circumstances tab      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Entry                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entry summary screen displays |
|                                   | the following table               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Entry type                    |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | Status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View entry screen will        |
|                                   | display                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Delete                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Delete? pop up notification   |
|                                   | will display                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the staff want to complete   |
|                                   | the Delete respite residential    |
|                                   | entry process?                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes                    |
|                                   | -   The Entry summary screen will |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   The entry event’s status in   |
|                                   |     the Entry summary screen will |
|                                   |     display as Deleted            |
|                                   | -   Staff must Add care recipient |
|                                   |     notes of Using the Aged Care  |
|                                   |     Staff Portal to manage care   |
|                                   |     recipient notes (Care         |
|                                   |     Recipient in Context (CRiC))  |
|                                   | -   Document clear and accurate   |
|                                   |     notes detailing the action    |
|                                   |     taken                         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Cancel and return to   |
|                                   |     the View entry screen         |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
