Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage enteral feeding events for residential care (Service in Context)

Table 18

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Home care enteral feeding events  |
|                                   | are managed in the Aged Care      |
|                                   | Management Payment System (ACMPS) |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See the Key enteral feeding   |
|                                   |     supplement application in     |
|                                   |     ACMPS table                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process table is about       |
|                                   | managing residential care enteral |
|                                   | feeding events in ACSP.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP service in context  |
|                                   | home page Service Officers must   |
|                                   | go to a care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   | page to manage enteral feeding.   |
|                                   | See Table 12, Step 2 for the      |
|                                   | process.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enteral feeding summary           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 2         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View enteral feeding              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 3         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enteral feeding event history     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 4         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register enteral feeding          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 5         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update enteral feeding            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 6         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Approve, delete or reject enteral |
|                                   | feeding events - go to Step 7     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enteral feeding documents         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 8         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to and using the Enteral    |
|                                   | feeding summary screen + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP service in context  |
|                                   | home page, Service Officers must  |
|                                   | go to a care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   | page to manage enteral feeding.   |
|                                   | See Table 12, Step 2 for the      |
|                                   | process.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All enteral feeding events are    |
|                                   | registered in an individual care  |
|                                   | recipient profile.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Enteral feeding summary |
|                                   | screen using any of the           |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Enteral feeding        |
|                                   |     summary under the Supplements |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Enteral feeding summary   |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type Enteral feeding summary  |
|                                   |     in the Quick find search bar  |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The Enteral feeding summary   |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Enteral feeding summary |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Enteral feeding summary       |
|                                   | screen displays the following:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ‘If a higher supplement   |
|                                   |     is claimed, costings are      |
|                                   |     required on a daily basis’    |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   Care recipient banner -       |
|                                   |     displays the Care recipient   |
|                                   |     ID, SPARC care recipient ID,  |
|                                   |     Date of birth, Record type,   |
|                                   |     Type of care and the Service  |
|                                   |     type                          |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding type          |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can also:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the hyperlinked Status |
|                                   |     and the View enteral feeding  |
|                                   |     screen displays. Go to Step 3 |
|                                   | -   select Back to profile and    |
|                                   |     the care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   select Register enteral       |
|                                   |     feeding and the Register      |
|                                   |     enteral feeding screen        |
|                                   |     displays. Go to Step 5        |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Going to and using the View       |
|                                   | enteral feeding screen + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers from the Aged    |
|                                   | Care Payments Team (Aged Care and |
|                                   | Allied Health Branch) with the    |
|                                   | following roles have the          |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | enteral feeding events with a     |
|                                   | Held status (Held enteral feeding |
|                                   | events):                          |

|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Enteral feeding notes      |
|                                   | section, Service Officers can     |
|                                   | type in a keyword in the Search   |
|                                   | bar to search for all records     |
|                                   | that contain the keyword          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the View enteral feeding    |
|                                   | screen by:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   selecting the hyperlinked     |
|                                   |     Status on the Enteral feeding |
|                                   |     summary screen                |
|                                   | -   the View enteral feeding      |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the View enteral feeding    |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View enteral feeding screen   |

|                                   | View enteral feeding              |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | -   Version                       |

|                                   | -   Event submission date         |
|                                   | -   Submitted by                  |
|                                   | -   Channel                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enteral feeding details           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding type          |
|                                   | -   Bolus - if applicable and     |
|                                   |     displays either Yes or No     |
|                                   | -   Net value - if applicable     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enteral feeding notes - will      |
|                                   | display notes if applicable       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Documents - displays relevant     |
|                                   | documents. Service Officers can   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | document to display the document  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the View enteral feeding     |
|                                   | screen, Service Officers can      |
|                                   | select:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event history to view the     |
|                                   |     Enteral feeding event history |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 4         |
|                                   | -   Go to enteral feeding summary |
|                                   |     to return to the Enteral      |
|                                   |     feeding summary screen        |
|                                   | -   Delete to delete the enteral  |
|                                   |     feeding event - go to Step 7  |
|                                   | -   Reject to reject the Held     |
|                                   |     enteral feeding event - go to |
|                                   |     Step 7                        |
|                                   | -   Go to enteral feeding         |
|                                   |     documents to display the      |
|                                   |     Enteral feeding documents     |
|                                   |     screen. Go to Step 8          |
|                                   | -   Update to update the enteral  |
|                                   |     feeding event - go to Step 6  |
|                                   | -   Approve to update the Held    |
|                                   |     enteral feeding event - go to |
|                                   |     Step 7                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Going to and using the Event      |
|                                   | history screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: The Event history screen    |
|                                   | will only display if updates or   |
|                                   | deletion have been made to an     |
|                                   | enteral feeding event.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Event history        |
|                                   | screen:                           |

|                                   | enteral feeding event.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Event history screen displays |
|                                   | the following information in a    |
|                                   | table format:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event ID                      |
|                                   | -   Version                       |

|                                   |     to display from the Show      |

|                                   |     screen)                       |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Going to and using the Register   |
|                                   | enteral feeding screen + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Register enteral     |
|                                   | feeding screen:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Register enteral       |
|                                   |     feeding on the Enteral        |
|                                   |     feeding summary screen        |
|                                   | -   The Register enteral feeding  |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Register enteral        |
|                                   | feeding screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All enteral feeding events    |
|                                   |     registered (created) in ACSP  |
|                                   |     will automatically have an    |
|                                   |     Accepted status               |
|                                   | -   The ‘You must sight the       |
|                                   |     enteral feeding supplement    |
|                                   |     (AC011) form, invoices and    |
|                                   |     medical certificate while     |
|                                   |     registering the enteral       |
|                                   |     feeding event’ information    |
|                                   |     message displays              |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can only     |
|                                   |     register an enteral feeding   |
|                                   |     event after assessing the     |
|                                   |     Application for Oxygen and    |
|                                   |     Enteral Feeding Supplement    |
|                                   |     (AC011) and medical           |
|                                   |     certificate(s) as complete.   |
|                                   |     See the Check application for |
|                                   |     oxygen and/or enteral feeding |
|                                   |     supplement is complete table  |
|                                   | -   Invoices must be provided for |
|                                   |     all higher enteral feeding    |
|                                   |     events                        |
|                                   | -   The Start date and End date   |
|                                   |     fields must be within the     |
|                                   |     care period                   |
|                                   | -   The Notes field has a 500     |
|                                   |     character limit               |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have the Oxygen and Enteral       |
|                                   | Feeding Supplement (AC011) form   |
|                                   | and medical certificate(s) been   |
|                                   | assessed as complete?             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, continue with this step  |
|                                   | -   No, Service Officers must     |
|                                   |     contact the service to        |
|                                   |     request missing information.  |
|                                   |     See the Check application for |
|                                   |     oxygen and/or enteral feeding |
|                                   |     supplement is complete table. |
|                                   |     Once complete documentation   |
|                                   |     is received, repeat Step 5    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register enteral feeding   |
|                                   | screen, complete the following    |
|                                   | fields:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Start date* field - key the date  |
|                                   | (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from the  |
|                                   | calendar (select the calendar     |
|                                   | icon to display the calendar)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | End date field - key the date     |
|                                   | (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from the  |
|                                   | calendar (select the calendar     |
|                                   | icon to display the calendar)     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Bolus - defaults to Yes.      |
|                                   |     Select No feeding type if     |
|                                   |     applicable                    |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding type* field   |
|                                   |      - defaults to Normal. Select |
|                                   |     Higher enteral feeding type   |
|                                   |     if applicable                 |
|                                   | -   Net Value* - will only        |
|                                   |     display if Higher feeding     |
|                                   |     type is selected. The Net     |
|                                   |     Value is (mls per day/Tin     |
|                                   |     size * Tin cost + Giving      |
|                                   |     set + Flexitainer + Hire of   |
|                                   |     pump cost)                    |
|                                   | -   Notes field - document clear  |
|                                   |     and accurate notes detailing  |
|                                   |     the action taken              |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 7                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To cancel at any time, select |
|                                   |     Cancel                        |
|                                   | -   Select Yes to cancel the      |
|                                   |     process                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Going to and using the Update     |
|                                   | enteral feeding screen + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Update enteral       |
|                                   | feeding screen:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Update on the View     |
|                                   |     enteral feeding screen        |
|                                   | -   The Update enteral feeding    |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Update enteral feeding  |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All enteral feeding events        |
|                                   | updated in ACSP will              |
|                                   | automatically have an Accepted    |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can only update  |
|                                   | an Enteral feeding event after    |
|                                   | assessing the Application for     |
|                                   | Oxygen and Enteral Feeding        |
|                                   | Supplement (AC011) and medical    |
|                                   | certificate(s) as complete. See   |
|                                   | the Check application for oxygen  |
|                                   | and/or enteral feeding supplement |
|                                   | is complete table for more        |
|                                   | information                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the update is for an existing  |
|                                   | enteral feeding event and the     |
|                                   | start date is prior to the        |
|                                   | original date, a new medical      |
|                                   | certificate must be provided      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event is for the higher    |
|                                   | enteral feeding rate, invoices    |
|                                   | must be provided                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When Service Officers are         |
|                                   | updating Notes, the updated       |
|                                   | information will display as an    |
|                                   | annotation                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   That is, the annotation (the  |
|                                   |     updated content) will display |
|                                   |     in additional to the original |
|                                   |     Notes information             |
|                                   | -   The annotation will not       |
|                                   |     override (replace) the        |
|                                   |     original Notes information    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To update the enteral feeding     |
|                                   | event:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the hyperlinked Status on  |
|                                   | the Enteral feeding summary       |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View enteral feeding screen   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Update                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Update enteral feeding screen |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key the relevant updates          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Start date* field - key the   |
|                                   |     date (DD.MM.YYYY), or select  |
|                                   |     from the calendar (select the |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   End date field - key the date |
|                                   |     (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from  |
|                                   |     the calendar (select the      |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   Bolus - defaults to the       |
|                                   |     original selection (either    |
|                                   |     Yes or No). Select the other  |
|                                   |     option if applicable          |
|                                   | -   Net Value - key in the higher |
|                                   |     amount of Enteral feeding     |
|                                   | -   Notes - document clear and    |
|                                   |     accurate reason for the       |
|                                   |     update                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Submit                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 7                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To cancel at any time select  |
|                                   |     Cancel                        |
|                                   | -   Select Yes to cancel the      |
|                                   |     process                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Approve, delete or reject an      |
|                                   | enteral feeding event + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An enteral feeding event can only |
|                                   | be approved or rejected after the |
|                                   | Application for Oxygen and        |
|                                   | Enteral Feeding Supplement        |
|                                   | (AC011) and medical               |
|                                   | certificate(s) have been assessed |
|                                   | as complete. See the Check        |
|                                   | application for oxygen and/or     |
|                                   | enteral feeding supplement is     |
|                                   | complete table for more           |
|                                   | information                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the application is for the     |
|                                   | higher enteral feeding rate       |
|                                   | invoices must be provided         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All enteral feeding events        |
|                                   | registered (created) and/or       |
|                                   | updated in ACSP will              |
|                                   | automatically have an Accepted    |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All enteral feeding events        |
|                                   | registered (created) and/or       |
|                                   | updated in the Aged Care Provider |
|                                   | Portal (ACPP) will automatically  |
|                                   | have a Held status                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SME and/or Team Leaders from the  |
|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |
|                                   | with the following roles have the |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | enteral feeding events with a     |
|                                   | Held status (Held enteral feeding |
|                                   | events):                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Service Officer     |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor security role         |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Approve a Held enteral feeding |
|                                   | event:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Approve on the View        |
|                                   | enteral feeding screen            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Approve? pop up notification  |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The successful receipt        |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   A summary of the enteral      |
|                                   |     feeding event                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to enteral feeding      |
|                                   | summary                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Enteral feeding summary       |
|                                   | screen displays and the enteral   |
|                                   | feeding event’s status is updated |
|                                   | to Accepted status                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Delete enteral feeding event:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Delete on the View enteral |
|                                   | feeding screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Delete? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Enteral feeding summary       |
|                                   | screen displays and the enteral   |
|                                   | feeding event’s status is updated |
|                                   | to Deleted status                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must Add care    |
|                                   | recipient notes of Using the Aged |
|                                   | Care Staff Portal to manage care  |
|                                   | recipient notes (Care Recipient   |
|                                   | in Context (CRiC))                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key clear and concise notes   |
|                                   |     of the action taken           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Reject a Held enteral feeding  |
|                                   | event:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Reject on the View enteral |
|                                   | feeding screen                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Reject? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key clear and accurate rejection  |
|                                   | reason in the Rejection reason    |
|                                   | section                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The successful receipt        |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   A summary of the enteral      |
|                                   |     feeding event including the   |
|                                   |     rejection reason              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to enteral feeding      |
|                                   | summary                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Enteral feeding summary       |
|                                   | screen displays and the enteral   |
|                                   | feeding event’s status is updated |
|                                   | to Rejected status                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Going to and using the Enteral    |
|                                   | feeding documents screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Enteral feeding      |
|                                   | documents screen:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Go to enteral feeding  |
|                                   |     documents on the View enteral |
|                                   |     feeding screen                |
|                                   | -   The Enteral feeding documents |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Enteral feeding         |
|                                   | documents screen                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must use the     |
|                                   | Enteral feeding documents screen  |
|                                   | to upload all relevant documents  |
|                                   | associated with the enteral       |
|                                   | feeding event.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | With the Enteral feeding          |
|                                   | documents screen, Service         |
|                                   | Officers may experience the       |
|                                   | following error messages when     |
|                                   | uploading documents:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘More than 10 files were      |
|                                   | selected for upload. Please       |
|                                   | select 10 files or less’ error    |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A maximum of 10 documents for |
|                                   |     each enteral feeding event    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘File type selected for       |
|                                   | upload is larger than 5MB. Please |
|                                   | select files smaller than 5MB’    |
|                                   | error message                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Each document must be smaller |
|                                   |     than 5 MB                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘File type selected for       |
|                                   | upload is not supported. Please   |
|                                   | select JPG, JPEG, TIFF, PNG and   |
|                                   | PDF file types only’ error        |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Each document must be         |
|                                   |     uploaded in the accepted file |
|                                   |     type                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘Response required’ error     |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A document type must be       |
|                                   |     selected from the drop down   |
|                                   |     menu                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must resolve the |
|                                   | error message before they can     |
|                                   | successfully upload documents.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Enteral feeding documents     |
|                                   | screen displays the following     |
|                                   | section:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding details       |
|                                   | -   Upload documents              |
|                                   | -   Documents                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Upload documents:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Select documents   |
|                                   |     option in the Upload          |
|                                   |     documents section             |
|                                   | -   The Open dialog box will      |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   Upload the relevant document  |
|                                   | -   Repeat this process for each  |
|                                   |     relevant document             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Upload documents     |
|                                   | process?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful information    |
|                                   |     message displays              |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can select   |
|                                   |     the relevant hyperlinked      |
|                                   |     document to display the       |
|                                   |     document                      |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, select either                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Remove and the uploaded       |
|                                   |     document is deleted or        |
|                                   | -   Go to enteral feeding         |
|                                   |     documents or Go to enteral    |
|                                   |     feeding summary or Go to      |
|                                   |     current claim. See the below  |
|                                   |     Notes                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When Service Officers select      |
|                                   | either Go to enteral feeding      |
|                                   | documents, Go to enteral feeding  |
|                                   | summary or Go to current claim,   |
|                                   | the Leave? pop up notification    |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes and the relevant screen   |
|                                   |     displays, or                  |
|                                   | -   No to remain on the Enteral   |
|                                   |     feeding documents screen      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Viewing the Receipt screen + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Receipt screen displays |
|                                   | when an enteral feeding event has |
|                                   | been created or updated.          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The successful receipt            |
|                                   | information message               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A summary of the enteral feeding  |
|                                   | event                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event status                  |
|                                   | -   Event submission date         |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Bolus                         |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding type - if     |
|                                   |     applicable                    |
|                                   | -   Net value - if applicable     |
|                                   | -   Enteral feeding notes         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to enteral feeding         |
|                                   |     documents to display the      |
|                                   |     Enteral feeding documents     |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Go to enteral feeding summary |
|                                   |     to return to the Enteral      |
|                                   |     feeding summary screen        |
|                                   | -   Go to current claim to return |
|                                   |     to the Current claim screen   |
