Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage oxygen events for residential care (Service in Context)

Table 19

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Home care oxygen events are       |
|                                   | managed in the Aged Care          |
|                                   | Management Payment System (ACMPS) |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See the Key oxygen supplement |
|                                   |     application in ACMPS table    |
|                                   |     for the process               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process table is about       |
|                                   | managing residential care oxygen  |
|                                   | events in ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP service in context  |
|                                   | home page Service Officers must   |
|                                   | go to a care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   | page to manage oxygen. See Table  |
|                                   | 12, Step 2 for the process.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Oxygen summary                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 2         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View oxygen                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 3         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Oxygen event history              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 4         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register oxygen                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 5         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Update oxygen                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 6         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Approve, delete or reject an      |
|                                   | oxygen event - go to Step 7       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Oxygen documents                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen - go to Step 8         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to and using the Oxygen     |
|                                   | summary screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP service in context  |
|                                   | home page Service Officers must   |
|                                   | go to a care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   | page to manage oxygen. See Table  |
|                                   | 12, Step 2 for the process.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All oxygen events are registered  |
|                                   | in an individual care recipient   |
|                                   | profile.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Oxygen summary screen   |
|                                   | using any of the following:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Oxygen summary under   |
|                                   |     the Supplements section       |
|                                   | -   The Oxygen summary screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Quick find navigation bar         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Type Oxygen summary in the    |
|                                   |     Quick find search bar         |
|                                   | -   Select Go                     |
|                                   | -   The Oxygen summary screen     |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Oxygen summary screen   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   | displays the following:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the ‘If a higher supplement   |
|                                   |     is claimed, costings are      |
|                                   |     required on a monthly basis’  |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   Care recipient banner -       |
|                                   |     displays the Care recipient   |
|                                   |     ID, SPARC care recipient ID,  |
|                                   |     Date of birth, Record type,   |
|                                   |     Type of care and the Service  |
|                                   |     type                          |
|                                   | -   Oxygen type                   |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Status                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can also:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select the hyperlinked Status |
|                                   |     and the View oxygen screen    |
|                                   |     displays. Go to Step 3        |
|                                   | -   select Back to profile and    |
|                                   |     the care recipient’s profile  |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   select Register Oxygen and    |
|                                   |     the Register Oxygen screen    |
|                                   |     displays. Go to Step 5        |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Going to and using the View       |
|                                   | oxygen screen + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Subject Matter Experts (SME)      |
|                                   | and/or Team Leaders from the Aged |
|                                   | Care Payments Team (Aged Care and |
|                                   | Allied Health Branch) have the    |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | oxygen events with a Held status  |
|                                   | (Held oxygen events):             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Service Officer     |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor security role         |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the View oxygen screen by:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   selecting the hyperlinked     |
|                                   |     Status on the Oxygen summary  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   the View oxygen screen        |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the View oxygen screen      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View oxygen screen displays   |
|                                   | the following information:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View Oxygen                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event ID                      |
|                                   | -   Version                       |
|                                   | -   Event status                  |
|                                   | -   Event submission date         |
|                                   | -   Submitted by                  |
|                                   | -   Channel                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Oxygen details                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Oxygen type - if applicable   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Oxygen notes - Service Officers   |
|                                   | can type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   | Search bar to search for all      |
|                                   | records that contain the keyword  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Documents - displays relevant     |
|                                   | documents. Service Officers can   |
|                                   | select the relevant hyperlinked   |
|                                   | document to display the document  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the View oxygen screen,      |
|                                   | Service Officers can also select: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event history to view the     |
|                                   |     Oxygen event history screen - |
|                                   |     go to Step 4                  |
|                                   | -   Go to oxygen summary to       |
|                                   |     return to the Oxygen summary  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Delete to delete the oxygen   |
|                                   |     event - go to Step 7          |
|                                   | -   Reject to reject the Held     |
|                                   |     oxygen event - go to Step 7   |
|                                   | -   Go to oxygen documents to     |
|                                   |     display the Oxygen documents  |
|                                   |     screen. Go to Step 8          |
|                                   | -   Update to update the oxygen   |
|                                   |     event - go to Step 6          |
|                                   | -   Approve to approve the Held   |
|                                   |     oxygen event - go to Step 7   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Going to and using the Event      |
|                                   | history screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Event history screen    |
|                                   | will only display if updates or   |
|                                   | deletions have been made to an    |
|                                   | oxygen event.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Event history        |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Event history on the   |
|                                   |     View oxygen screen            |
|                                   | -   The Event history screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Event history screen    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Event history screen displays |
|                                   | the change history for a specific |
|                                   | oxygen event.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Event history screen displays |
|                                   | the following information in a    |
|                                   | table format:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event ID                      |
|                                   | -   Version                       |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   | -   Channel                       |
|                                   | -   Event type                    |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Submitted by                  |
|                                   | -   Status - select the           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Status to display |
|                                   |     the relevant change details   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Back to return to the  |
|                                   |     View oxygen screen            |
|                                   | -   type in a keyword in the      |
|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |
|                                   | -   select the number of records  |
|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Going to and using the Register   |
|                                   | oxygen screen + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Register oxygen      |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Register oxygen on the |
|                                   |     Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   | -   The Register oxygen screen    |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Register oxygen        |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   All oxygen events registered  |
|                                   |     (created) in ACSP will        |
|                                   |     automatically have an         |
|                                   |     Accepted status               |
|                                   | -   The ‘You must sight the       |
|                                   |     oxygen supplement (AC011)     |
|                                   |     form, invoices and medical    |
|                                   |     certificate while registering |
|                                   |     the oxygen event’ information |
|                                   |     message displays              |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can only     |
|                                   |     register an oxygen event      |
|                                   |     after assessing the           |
|                                   |     Application for Oxygen and    |
|                                   |     Enteral Feeding Supplement    |
|                                   |     (AC011) and medical           |
|                                   |     certificate(s) as complete.   |
|                                   |     See the Check application for |
|                                   |     oxygen and/or enteral feeding |
|                                   |     supplement is complete table  |
|                                   |     for more information          |
|                                   | -   Invoices must be provided for |
|                                   |     all higher oxygen events      |
|                                   | -   The Start date and End date   |
|                                   |     fields must be within the     |
|                                   |     care period                   |
|                                   | -   The Notes field has a 500     |
|                                   |     character limit               |
|                                   | -   All fields are optional       |
|                                   |     unless marked with an         |
|                                   |     asterisk                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Have the Oxygen and Enteral       |
|                                   | Feeding Supplement (AC011) and    |
|                                   | medical certificate been assessed |
|                                   | as complete?                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, continue with this step  |
|                                   | -   No, Service Officers must     |
|                                   |     contact the service to        |
|                                   |     request missing information.  |
|                                   |     See the Check application for |
|                                   |     oxygen and/or enteral feeding |
|                                   |     supplement is complete table  |
|                                   |     for more information. Once    |
|                                   |     complete documentation is     |
|                                   |     received, repeat Step 5       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Register oxygen screen,    |
|                                   | complete the following fields:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Start date* field - key the   |
|                                   |     date (DD.MM.YYYY), or select  |
|                                   |     from the calendar (select the |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   End date field - key the date |
|                                   |     (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from  |
|                                   |     the calendar (select the      |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   Oxygen type* field  -         |
|                                   |     defaults to Normal. Select    |
|                                   |     Higher if applicable          |
|                                   | -   Net Value* - will only        |
|                                   |     display if Higher oxygen type |
|                                   |     is selected. The net value =  |
|                                   |     (Concentrator hire + Cylinder |
|                                   |     Delivery cost + Cylinder      |
|                                   |     Hire + Kit Hire)              |
|                                   | -   Notes field - document clear  |
|                                   |     and accurate notes detailing  |
|                                   |     the action taken              |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Go to Step 7                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To cancel at any time, select |
|                                   |     Cancel                        |
|                                   | -   Select Yes to cancel the      |
|                                   |     process                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Going to and using the Update     |
|                                   | oxygen screen + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Update oxygen        |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   select Update on the View     |
|                                   |     oxygen screen                 |
|                                   | -   the Update oxygen screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the Update oxygen screen    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All oxygen events updated in ACSP |
|                                   | will automatically have an        |
|                                   | Accepted status                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can only update  |
|                                   | an oxygen event after assessing   |
|                                   | the Application for Oxygen and    |
|                                   | Enteral Feeding Supplement        |
|                                   | (AC011) and medical               |
|                                   | certificate(s) as complete. See   |
|                                   | the Check application for oxygen  |
|                                   | and/or enteral feeding supplement |
|                                   | is complete table for more        |
|                                   | information                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the update is for an existing  |
|                                   | oxygen event and the start date   |
|                                   | is before the original date, a    |
|                                   | new medical certificate must be   |
|                                   | provided                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event is for the higher    |
|                                   | oxygen rate, invoices must be     |
|                                   | provided                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When Service Officers are         |
|                                   | updating Notes, the updated       |
|                                   | information will display as an    |
|                                   | annotation                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   That is, the annotation (the  |
|                                   |     updated content) will display |
|                                   |     in additional to the original |
|                                   |     Notes information             |
|                                   | -   The annotation will not       |
|                                   |     override (replace) the        |
|                                   |     original Notes information    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All fields are optional unless    |
|                                   | marked with an asterisk           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Update the oxygen event:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the hyperlinked Status on  |
|                                   | the Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen details screen         |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Update                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Update oxygen screen displays |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key the relevant updates          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Start date* field - key the   |
|                                   |     date (DD.MM.YYYY), or select  |
|                                   |     from the calendar (select the |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   End date field - key the date |
|                                   |     (DD.MM.YYYY), or select from  |
|                                   |     the calendar (select the      |
|                                   |     calendar icon to display the  |
|                                   |     calendar)                     |
|                                   | -   Net Value - key in the higher |
|                                   |     amount of oxygen              |
|                                   | -   Notes - document clear and    |
|                                   |     accurate reason for the       |
|                                   |     update                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Submit                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 9                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   To cancel at any time select  |
|                                   |     Cancel                        |
|                                   | -   Select Yes to cancel the      |
|                                   |     process                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Approve, delete or reject an      |
|                                   | oxygen event + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An oxygen event can only be       |
|                                   | approved or rejected after the    |
|                                   | Application for Oxygen and        |
|                                   | Enteral Feeding Supplement        |
|                                   | (AC011), and medical certificate  |
|                                   | have been assessed as complete.   |
|                                   | See the Check application for     |
|                                   | oxygen and/or enteral feeding     |
|                                   | supplement is complete table for  |
|                                   | more information                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the event is for the higher    |
|                                   | oxygen rate, invoices must be     |
|                                   | provided                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All oxygen events registered      |
|                                   | (created) and/or updated in ACSP  |
|                                   | will automatically have an        |
|                                   | Accepted status                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | All oxygen events registered      |
|                                   | (created) and/or updated in the   |
|                                   | Aged Care Provider Portal (ACPP)  |
|                                   | will automatically have a Held    |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SME and/or Team Leaders from the  |
|                                   | Aged Care Payments Team (Aged     |
|                                   | Care and Allied Health Branch)    |
|                                   | with the following roles have the |
|                                   | authority to approve or reject    |
|                                   | oxygen events with a Held status  |
|                                   | (Held oxygen events)              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Service Officer     |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   | -   Aged Care Technical Program   |
|                                   |     Advisor security role         |
|                                   | -   Business Administrator        |
|                                   |     security role                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Approve a Held oxygen event:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Approve on the View oxygen |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Approve? pop up notification  |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The successful receipt        |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   A summary of the oxygen event |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to oxygen summary       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   | displays and the oxygen event’s   |
|                                   | status is updated to Accepted     |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Delete an oxygen event:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Delete on the View oxygen  |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Delete? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   | displays and the oxygen event’s   |
|                                   | status is updated to Deleted      |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must Add care    |
|                                   | recipient notes                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Key clear and concise notes   |
|                                   |     of the action taken           |
|                                   | -   See Using the Aged Care Staff |
|                                   |     Portal to manage care         |
|                                   |     recipient notes (Care         |
|                                   |     Recipient in Context (CRiC))  |
|                                   |     for the process               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Reject a Held oxygen event:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Reject on the View oxygen  |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Reject? pop up notification   |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key clear and accurate rejection  |
|                                   | reason in the Rejection reason    |
|                                   | section                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Yes                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The successful receipt        |
|                                   |     information message           |
|                                   | -   A summary of the oxygen event |
|                                   |     including the rejection       |
|                                   |     reason                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Go to oxygen summary       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen summary screen         |
|                                   | displays and the oxygen event’s   |
|                                   | status is updated to Rejected     |
|                                   | status                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Going to and using the Oxygen     |
|                                   | documents screen + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To go to the Oxygen documents     |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Go to oxygen documents |
|                                   |     on the View oxygen screen     |
|                                   | -   The Oxygen documents screen   |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To use the Oxygen documents       |
|                                   | screen                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must use the     |
|                                   | Oxygen documents screen to upload |
|                                   | all relevant documents associated |
|                                   | with the oxygen event.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | With the Oxygen documents screen, |
|                                   | Service Officers may experience   |
|                                   | the following error messages when |
|                                   | uploading documents:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘More than 10 files were      |
|                                   | selected for upload. Please       |
|                                   | select 10 files or less’ error    |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A maximum of 10 documents for |
|                                   |     each oxygen event             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘File type selected for       |
|                                   | upload is larger than 5MB. Please |
|                                   | select files smaller than 5MB’    |
|                                   | error message                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Each document must be smaller |
|                                   |     than 5 MB                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘File type selected for       |
|                                   | upload is not supported. Please   |
|                                   | select JPG, JPEG, TIFF, PNG and   |
|                                   | PDF file types only’ error        |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Each document must be         |
|                                   |     uploaded in the accepted file |
|                                   |     type                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘Response required’ error     |
|                                   | message                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   A document type must be       |
|                                   |     selected from the drop down   |
|                                   |     menu                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers must resolve the |
|                                   | error message before they can     |
|                                   | successfully upload documents.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Oxygen documents screen       |
|                                   | displays the following section:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Oxygen details                |
|                                   | -   Upload documents              |
|                                   | -   Documents - displays          |
|                                   |     documents uploaded by either  |
|                                   |     ‘A users’ in the Aged Care    |
|                                   |     Provider Portal or Service    |
|                                   |     Officers in ACSP              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To Upload documents:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Select documents   |
|                                   |     option in the Upload          |
|                                   |     documents section             |
|                                   | -   The Open dialog box will      |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   | -   Upload the relevant document  |
|                                   | -   Repeat this process for each  |
|                                   |     relevant document             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Upload documents     |
|                                   | process?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   The successful information    |
|                                   |     message displays              |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can select   |
|                                   |     the relevant hyperlinked      |
|                                   |     document to display the       |
|                                   |     document                      |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Remove and the         |
|                                   |     uploaded document is deleted  |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   Select either Go to oxygen    |
|                                   |     details, Go to oxygen summary |
|                                   |     or Go to current claim        |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   See the below Notes           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can also select  |
|                                   | either Go to oxygen details, Go   |
|                                   | to oxygen summary or Go to        |
|                                   | current claim details             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Leave? pop up notification    |
|                                   | displays                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Yes and the relevant   |
|                                   |     screen displays, or           |
|                                   | -   Select No to remain on the    |
|                                   |     Oxygen documents screen       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Viewing the Receipt screen + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note: the Receipt screen displays |
|                                   | when an oxygen event has been     |
|                                   | created or updated.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Receipt screen displays the   |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The successful receipt            |
|                                   | information message               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A summary of the oxygen event     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Event status                  |
|                                   | -   Event submission date         |
|                                   | -   Start date                    |
|                                   | -   End date                      |
|                                   | -   Oxygen type - if applicable   |
|                                   | -   Net value - if applicable     |
|                                   | -   Oxygen notes                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to oxygen summary to       |
|                                   |     return to the Oxygen summary  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Go to current claim to return |
|                                   |     to the Current claim screen   |
|                                   | -   Go to oxygen documents to     |
|                                   |     display the Oxygen documents  |
|                                   |     screen                        |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to view additional Transition Care days (Service in Context)

Table 20

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Options + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This process table applies to     |
|                                   | residential care services only    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See Manage aged care          |
|                                   |     recipient details to view the |
|                                   |     details for home care         |
|                                   |     recipients                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can use this     |
|                                   | process table to view a care      |
|                                   | recipient’s additional transition |
|                                   | care days in the Aged Care Staff  |
|                                   | Portal (ACSP).                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following         |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional transition care days   |
|                                   | summary                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to the screen - go to   |
|                                   |     Step 2                        |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen - go to    |
|                                   |     Step 3                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | View additional transition care   |
|                                   | days                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Viewing the screen - go to    |
|                                   |     Step 4                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to the Additional           |
|                                   | transition care days summary      |
|                                   | screen + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |
|                                   | home page, go to the Additional   |
|                                   | transition care days summary      |
|                                   | screen using any of the           |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Main menu (Hamburger button)      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) under the Service   |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   Complete the Care recipient   |
|                                   |     search screen                 |
|                                   | -   Select Search to generate the |
|                                   |     search results                |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Care recipient ID |
|                                   |     to display the Care recipient |
|                                   |     service entries screen        |
|                                   | -   select Transition care under  |
|                                   |     the Additional days section   |
|                                   | -   the Additional transition     |
|                                   |     care days summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional days menu tab          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) under the Service   |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The Care recipient search     |
|                                   |     screen displays               |
|                                   | -   Complete the Care recipient   |
|                                   |     search screen                 |
|                                   | -   Select Search to generate the |
|                                   |     search results                |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Care recipient ID |
|                                   |     to display the Care recipient |
|                                   |     service entries screen        |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Service NAPS ID   |
|                                   |     to display the Care recipient |
|                                   |     summary (all services) screen |
|                                   | -   Hover the mouse pointer over  |
|                                   |     the Additional days menu tab  |
|                                   | -   A pop up window will display  |
|                                   | -   Select Transition care        |
|                                   | -   The Additional transition     |
|                                   |     care days summary screen      |
|                                   |     displays                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Viewing the Additional transition |
|                                   | care days summary screen + Read   |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Additional transition     |
|                                   |     care days summary screen is a |
|                                   |     view only screen              |
|                                   | -   The No records available      |
|                                   |     information message will      |
|                                   |     display for care recipients   |
|                                   |     who have never had any        |
|                                   |     additional transition care    |
|                                   |     days recorded for them        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When the Department of Health and |
|                                   | Aged Care approves additional     |
|                                   | transition care days for a care   |
|                                   | recipient, this information is    |
|                                   | sent automatically to Services    |
|                                   | Australia via the NSAF gateway.   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Additional transition care    |
|                                   | days summary screen displays the  |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The ‘The additional days          |
|                                   | displayed are for the selected    |
|                                   | care recipient and not limited to |
|                                   | the service in context’           |
|                                   | information message               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care Recipient banner - displays  |
|                                   | the care recipient’s name, IDs,   |
|                                   | Date of Birth, Record type and    |
|                                   | Type of care status               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Additional transition care days   |
|                                   | table                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Reference ID                  |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Additional days               |
|                                   | -   Source                        |
|                                   | -   Created date                  |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Action - displays either      |
|                                   |     Created or Updated. Service   |
|                                   |     Officers can select the       |
|                                   |     hyperlinked Status to display |
|                                   |     the individual record         |
|                                   |     details. Go to Step 4         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select the   |
|                                   | number of records to display from |
|                                   | the Show records drop down list   |
|                                   | (bottom left corner of the        |
|                                   | screen).                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Viewing the View additional       |
|                                   | transition care days screen +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the Department of Health   |
|                                   |     and Aged Care updates an      |
|                                   |     individual record, the        |
|                                   |     Version details will change   |
|                                   |     and there are no changes to   |
|                                   |     the Reference ID. That is,    |
|                                   |     the Reference ID remains the  |
|                                   |     same throughout all updates   |
|                                   | -   If the Department of Health   |
|                                   |     and Aged Care has deleted an  |
|                                   |     individual additional         |
|                                   |     transition care days record,  |
|                                   |     this record will no longer    |
|                                   |     display in the Additional     |
|                                   |     transition care days summary  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To view an individual additional  |
|                                   | transition care days record on    |
|                                   | the Additional transition care    |
|                                   | days summary screen:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the hyperlinked Status in  |
|                                   | the Additional transition care    |
|                                   | days table                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The View additional transition    |
|                                   | care days screen displays the     |
|                                   | following                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Care Recipient banner -       |
|                                   |     displays the care recipient’s |
|                                   |     name, IDs, Date of Birth,     |
|                                   |     Record type and Type of care  |
|                                   |     status                        |
|                                   | -   Version                       |
|                                   | -   Action                        |
|                                   | -   Source                        |
|                                   | -   Last updated                  |
|                                   | -   Channel                       |
|                                   | -   Reference ID                  |
|                                   | -   Entry date                    |
|                                   | -   Number of additional days     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can select Close |
|                                   | and the Additional transition     |
|                                   | care days summary screen will     |
|                                   | display.                          |

Using the Aged Care Staff Portal to manage Aged Care Funding Instruments (ACFIs) (Service in Context)

Table 22

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Menu options available in the     |
|                                   | Aged Care Staff Portal (ACSP) +   |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | PDF format of the Aged Care       |
|                                   | Funding Instruments (ACFIs) is    |
|                                   | not available in ACSP             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   See the Resources page for a  |
|                                   |     manual workaround to this     |
|                                   |     issue                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The viewing of ACFI information   |
|                                   | for the period of 2008 to 2013 is |
|                                   | not available in ACSP             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must use     |
|                                   |     SPARC to view ACFI            |
|                                   |     information for this period   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The viewing of Resident           |
|                                   | Classification Scale (RCS)        |
|                                   | information is not available in   |
|                                   | ACSP                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   RCS was the funding model     |
|                                   |     arrangement before ACFI       |
|                                   | -   Service Officers must use     |
|                                   |     SPARC to view RCS information |
|                                   |     (pre-ACFI assessment          |
|                                   |     information)                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Use this process table to manage  |
|                                   | Aged Care Funding Instruments     |
|                                   | (ACFIs) in the Aged Care Staff    |
|                                   | Portal (ACSP). This process table |
|                                   | applies to residential care       |
|                                   | services only.                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Log on to ACSP.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Choose from the following menu    |
|                                   | options:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | ACFI summary                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen, go to Step 2          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     screens, go to Step 3         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Register ACFI                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Going to and using the        |
|                                   |     screen, go to Step 4          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | go to Step 5                      |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | update an Accepted ACFI - go to   |
|                                   | Step 6                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Going to and using the ACFI       |
|                                   | summary screen + Read more ...    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the ACSP Service in Context  |

|                                   | -   Select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) to display the Care |
|                                   |     recipient search screen       |
|                                   | -   Key the care recipient’s      |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   Select Search to display the  |
|                                   |     care recipient profile        |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select ACFI summary under the |
|                                   |     Funding classifications       |
|                                   |     section                       |
|                                   | -   The ACFI summary screen will  |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Funding classifications menu tab  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Main menu icon     |
|                                   | -   Select Care recipient search  |
|                                   |     (service) to display the Care |
|                                   |     recipient search screen       |
|                                   | -   Key the care recipient’s      |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   Select Search to display the  |
|                                   |     care recipient profile        |

|                                   |     the Funding classifications   |
|                                   |     menu tab                      |
