|                                   | -   The ACFI summary screen will  |
|                                   |     display                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the ACFI summary screen     |

|                                   | Note: the No records available    |

|                                   | assessment.                       |

|                                   | Type of care status               |

|                                   | (ACFI) summary table              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Received date                 |
|                                   | -   Effective date                |
|                                   | -   Reason                        |
|                                   | -   Daily living                  |
|                                   | -   Behaviour                     |
|                                   | -   Complex health care           |

|                                   |     display. Go to Step 4         |

|                                   |     status to make changes to     |
|                                   |     draft ACFI. Go to Step 5      |

|                                   |     Search bar to search for all  |
|                                   |     records that contain the      |
|                                   |     keyword                       |

|                                   |     to display from the Show      |
|                                   |     records drop down list        |
|                                   |     (bottom left corner of the    |
|                                   |     screen)                       |

| 3                                 | Going to and viewing the View     |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Going to and using the Register   |
|                                   | ACFI screen + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     information                   |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Different sections of each        |

|                                   |     Mobility                      |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 3:       |
|                                   |     Personal hygiene              |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 4:       |
|                                   |     Toileting                     |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 5:       |
|                                   |     Continence                    |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 6:       |
|                                   |     Cognitive skills              |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 7:       |
|                                   |     Wandering                     |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 8:       |
|                                   |     Verbal behaviour              |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 9:       |
|                                   |     Physical behaviour            |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 10:      |
|                                   |     Depression                    |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 11:      |
|                                   |     Medication                    |
|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 12:      |
|                                   |     Complex health care           |

|                                   | Register ACFI - Verification      |
|                                   | screen will display.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers review all the   |
|                                   | ACFI questions by selecting ACFI  |
|                                   | hyperlinked questions on the      |
|                                   | Register ACFI - Verification.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer want to  |
|                                   | complete the Register ACFI        |
|                                   | process?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select Submit                 |
|                                   | -   Procedure ends here           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, select either:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Back to return to the         |
|                                   |     Register ACFI - ACFI 12:      |
|                                   |     Complex health care screen    |
|                                   | -   Cancel to cancel the Register |
|                                   |     ACFI process                  |
|                                   | -   Delete to delete the Register |
|                                   |     ACFI process                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can also select  |
|                                   | on each Register ACFI screen:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Cancel,                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   The Cancel? pop up            |
|                                   |     notification will display     |
|                                   | -   Select Yes and the ACFI’s     |
|                                   |     status remains as Draft and   |
|                                   |     only the information entered  |
|                                   |     at the point of the Cancel    |
|                                   |     request will be lost          |
|                                   |     (cancelled)                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Save and next to progress to the  |
|                                   | next Register ACFI screen         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Save and exit to return to the    |
|                                   | Aged Care Funding Instrument      |
|                                   | (ACFI) summary screen             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |

| 6                                 | Update a draft ACFI + Read more   |

|                                   |     information                   |

|                                   | status (Draft ACFI)               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | When Service Officers have        |

|                                   | ACFI category score               |

|                                   | -   Register ACFI - ACFI 7:       |

|                                   | screen.                           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   | No, select either:                |
